## Jedi

## Historical information

### Date founded

c. [25,025 BBY](/wiki/25,025_BBY "25,025 BBY"), on [Ahch-To](/wiki/Ahch-To "Ahch-To")[[20]](#cite_note-Timelines_date-20)

### Founder

[Prime Jedi](/wiki/Prime_Jedi "Prime Jedi")[[6]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-6)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Religion)

:   "*For over a thousand generations, the Jedi knights were the guardians of peace and justice in the old Republic. Before the dark times, before the Empire.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Luke Skywalker[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4)

A **Jedi**, often called a Jedi Knight, was a devotee to the ways of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"), an ancient order of [protectors](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") united by their [ability](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") to harness the [power](/wiki/Force_power "Force power") of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"). Adhering to a [doctrine](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code") that favored the [light side of the Force](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force"), the Jedi aspired to attain a state of inner tranquility through calmness and [meditation](/wiki/Meditation "Meditation") while avoiding emotions affiliated with the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"), such as anger and hatred. Nevertheless, Jedi philosophy did not forbid a Jedi from acting in self-defense or in the defense of others, and they were colloquially known as **Space Wizards** to citizens of [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy"). To that end, a Jedi's only possession was their [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber"), a symbol of their role as guardians of peace and justice.

Before the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), Jedi worked with the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") with a commitment to freedom and [democracy](/wiki/Democracy "Democracy"). The Jedi and the Republic's ideals brought them into [conflict](/wiki/Jedi-Sith_War "Jedi-Sith War") with an order of dark side wielders known as the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith"), who sought power and dominion over [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy"). Emerging victorious from their wars with the ancient Sith, the Jedi carried on in their duty as peacekeepers for over a [millennium](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium") until the [advent](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") of the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars") [twenty-two years](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY") before the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin"). Faced with a pan-[galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") civil war between the Republic and [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"), the Jedi adopted the mantle of [generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") and [soldiers](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier") in the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic"). After three [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") of conflict, the Jedi discovered that the Sith had deceived them and engineered the war to restore them back to power. However, just before the Sith were defeated, the Jedi were betrayed by one of their own—the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One") [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), who had been seduced to the dark side and anointed [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Vader by the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"). Using the Jedi's own [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") to initiate a [systematic purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") of the Jedi Order, the [Lords](/wiki/Lord "Lord") of the Sith all but [eradicated](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") the Jedi in one fell swoop, reducing the order from thousands of Jedi Knights guarding the galaxy, to a handful of survivors cast into [exile](/wiki/Exile_(punishment) "Exile (punishment)") across the galaxy.

The Sith ruled the galaxy through the Empire for a [generation](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"), but did not succeed in completely wiping out the Jedi Order. As a result, [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger") and [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker") were, in turn, [trained](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") as new Jedi by [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus") and [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"), respectively. Skywalker, the son of Vader, was also taught the ways of the Jedi by [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") and fought for the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") during the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War"). On his [death](/wiki/Death "Death") bed, Yoda gave his final apprentice the mandate of passing on his lessons to a new generation of Jedi. [Shortly afterward](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"), Skywalker succeeded in redeeming his [father](/wiki/Parent "Parent"), who sacrificed himself to save his son by killing his [Sith Master](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master"), [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") Sidious, thereby destroying the Sith and fulfilling the prophecy of the Chosen One.

During the [era](/wiki/New_Republic_era "New Republic era") of the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"), Skywalker worked to rebuild the Jedi Order by training a dozen apprentices, including his young but powerful nephew, [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo"), but Solo fell to the dark side and became Kylo Ren, apprentice of [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke"), [master](/wiki/Ren "Ren") of the [Knights of Ren](/wiki/Knights_of_Ren "Knights of Ren"), and a [warlord](/wiki/Warlord "Warlord") of the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order"), while [Skywalker's training temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_of_Luke_Skywalker "Jedi Temple of Luke Skywalker") and students were [destroyed](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Destruction of the Jedi Temple"). As the First Order [rose to power](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War"), Ren and Snoke sought to destroy Skywalker, who, in self-exile, briefly trained [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") in the ways of the Jedi until he sacrificed himself to save the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance"), after which time Skywalker's sister, [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"), continued her training. When a [reborn](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") Darth Sidious—Rey's grandfather—revealed himself to the galaxy, Ben Solo, the opposite in a [dyad in the Force](/wiki/Force_dyad "Force dyad") with Rey, was redeemed, and Rey sacrificed herself to [destroy](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol") the phantom Sith Lord, preventing the rebirth of the Sith Order. Rey was saved from death by Solo, who gave his life for hers, allowing the Jedi to live on.

## Description

### Philosophy

:   "*In order to master the ways of the Force, Jedi must forgo all attachment.*"
:   ―[The Armorer](/wiki/The_Armorer "The Armorer")[[21]](#cite_note-Boba_Chapter_5-21)

 [![To be a Jedi was to live a life of selflessness and devotion to the light side of the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/JediSitsAlone-InnerJedi.png/revision/latest?cb=20250807005626) [![To be a Jedi was to live a life of selflessness and devotion to the light side of the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/JediSitsAlone-InnerJedi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250807005626)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/JediSitsAlone-InnerJedi.png/revision/latest?cb=20250807005626) 

To be a Jedi was to live a life of selflessness and devotion to the light side of the Force.

 

The [Jedi Knights](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") focused on calmness and peace to channel their [powers](/wiki/Force_power "Force power") in [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"), using the [light side of the Force](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force") to serve in the capacity of guardians of peace and justice in [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy").[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4) Even so, the Jedi sought to preserve balance in the Force; the ancient prophecy of the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One") foretold of a being who would restore balance to the Force by destroying the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith"). In combat, whereas an enemy may grow impatient and rely on their overwhelming strength, a Jedi would [meditate](/wiki/Meditation "Meditation") and find serenity in their [mind](/wiki/Brain "Brain") to focus.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1) A Jedi used the Force for defense and knowledge rather than use it to gain power over others.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_V-2) Their chosen weapon the [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber"), a weapon with limitations, likewise symbolized the care a Jedi took wielding their gifts and that when a Jedi fights it is with intention and precision, ending conflict while injuring no more, or taking no more life, than the lightsaber's wielder chooses. [[22]](#cite_note-22) Always supposed to put the needs of others before their own,[[23]](#cite_note-Path_of_Ven-23) a Jedi was supposed to be selfless[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) and work to save others above themselves.[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24) Like all people, Jedi were imperfect and always needed to strive to better themselves, meaning it was impossible to be a "perfect Jedi."[[25]](#cite_note-Convergence-25)

Because of their ability in the Force, a Jedi, even if they lacked a physical weapon, was never defenseless,[[26]](#cite_note-Ahsoka_novel-26) and some Jedi were capable of appearing after [death](/wiki/Death "Death") as [Force spirits](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit").[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_V-2)[[27]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-27)[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-11) The Jedi considered themselves instruments of the Force,[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4) and during the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"), peacekeepers instead of [soldiers](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier").[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_II-5) Striving to be majestic yet simple,[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24) knowledge, the Force, and self-discipline were considered the three pillars of Jedi strength.[[28]](#cite_note-Complete_Visual_New-28) Instead of acting for selfish aims,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) such as securing wealth or power, the Jedi focused their pursuits on learning, reaching enlightenment,[[23]](#cite_note-Path_of_Ven-23) helping others[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) in a just fashion,[[25]](#cite_note-Convergence-25) and finding balance.[[29]](#cite_note-Age_Qui-Gon-29) The Jedi believed that—no matter one's physical appearance—everyone was internally made up of light. Individuals who did not understand the Force took to calling Jedi "space wizards."[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24)

Through the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") all Jedi belonged to, a Jedi was connected to the entire [galaxy](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy").[[25]](#cite_note-Convergence-25) As part of the Order, a single Jedi had the advantage of a structured community to rely on and gain confidence from.[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24) In the opinion of [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Matthea Cathley](/wiki/Matthea_Cathley "Matthea Cathley"), the Jedi were better as a group than on their own.[[23]](#cite_note-Path_of_Ven-23) Similarly, Jedi Knight [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") thought of the Order as something that proved that, in being a Jedi, he was part of something bigger than himself.[[30]](#cite_note-Obi-Wan_and_Anakin_5-30) Indeed, the Jedi could rely on their Order in tough times, enabling an individual Jedi to act in a bold fashion and make large scale choices about spreading light. One enemy of the Jedi, [Eye of the Nihil](/wiki/Eye_of_the_Nihil "Eye of the Nihil") [Marchion Ro](/wiki/Marchion_Ro "Marchion Ro"), thus regarded the Jedi Order as something the Jedi would tap into, much like their ability to tap into the Force itself.[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24)

The life of a Jedi was full of hardships. [Training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") to become a Jedi was difficult, according to [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn"), and those who succeeded were faced with a hard life ahead.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1) Adherence to the Jedi way required a disciplined mind and a strong sense of commitment, and it was considered unbecoming of a Jedi to seek adventure or excitement.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_V-2) The [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code") therefore regulated the lives of individual Jedi, their actions and beliefs, and the policies of the Jedi Order. While the Code permitted compassion, attachment and possession were forbidden to the Jedi.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_II-5) The Jedi believed that attachment led to jealousy, and greed in turn, and ultimately the fear of loss which was a pathway to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force").[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) Through the Force, the Jedi hoped to direct themselves through their passions, instead of acting in an impulsive manner.[[31]](#cite_note-Path_of_Deceit-31) Forgoing attachment was also considered essential to a Jedi's progress in mastering their [Force powers](/wiki/Force_power "Force power"),[[21]](#cite_note-Boba_Chapter_5-21) as their training could last from [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") to a lifetime.[[32]](#cite_note-Boba_Chapter_6-32) Despite the importance of non-attachment in the Jedi vow, there was disagreement on what that specifically meant.[[33]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-33)

Some Jedi took it to mean they needed to suppress their emotions, such as vanquishing love and discomfort from themselves, whereas others believed trying to master emotion went against the ideals of the Order. For the latter group of Jedi, emotions like love were centered upon the idea of letting go. Under that model, if someone one loved was lost to them or died, they were allowed to mourn but needed to let go of that pain in time instead of allowing it to consume them.[[33]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-33) Indeed, the Jedi accepted death as a part of the natural course of life, believing that the deceased should be celebrated instead of mourned for becoming one with the Force.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) Detachment was nonetheless one of the most difficult lessons for Jedi to learn, as it took practice and repetition to master. Learning the lesson—that, to be a Jedi, one needed to "let go"—multiple times over his long life,[[33]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-33) [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") was able to carry the belief to his deathbed after a lifespan of nine [centuries](/wiki/Standard_century "Standard century"), even accepting his death—the death of all life—as the way of the Force.[[34]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-34)

Indeed, the Jedi understood feelings like love to be natural; Jedi were allowed to feel these emotions,[[35]](#cite_note-The_Rise_of_Clovis-35) but their task was to balance their strong feelings.[[33]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-33) With an understanding of their strongest emotions, it was hoped a Jedi would analyze what, deep down, made them feel the way they did. Able to then address their underlining motivations, the Jedi could formulate the best possible path forward instead of allowing themself to act without thinking. Attachments like romance were understood to be distractions from the Jedi mission of spreading justice and the light side: it represented a person tying themself down to one attachment, rather than opening themself up to the galaxy as a whole. Bound only to the Force and the Jedi Temple, relationships to a Jedi needed to be carefully handled in the name of their service to the Force.[[31]](#cite_note-Path_of_Deceit-31) Close friendships still existed and were valued,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) but a Jedi needed to understand their friends could be lost and need to be let go of at any given time.[[33]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-33)

### Galactic sentiments

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Anti-Jedi sentiment](/wiki/Anti-Jedi_sentiment "Anti-Jedi sentiment")

:   "*People made holodramas about them, wrote stories. The Jedi were…*celebrities*, and rightly so.*"
:   ―[The Archivist](/wiki/The_Archivist "The Archivist")[[36]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_3-36)

 [![Throughout galactic history, anti-Jedi sentiment appeared amongst certain groups.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d0/Dont_Believe_the_Lies.png/revision/latest?cb=20250106004758) [![Throughout galactic history, anti-Jedi sentiment appeared amongst certain groups.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d0/Dont_Believe_the_Lies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250106004758)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d0/Dont_Believe_the_Lies.png/revision/latest?cb=20250106004758) 

Throughout galactic history, anti-Jedi sentiment appeared amongst certain groups.

 

Throughout the [history of the galaxy](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history"), Jedi were often seen as a noble order that protected the galaxy and the [Galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") Republic as the guardians of peace and justice.[[37]](#cite_note-DB:Order-37) In some cases, like [Onderonians](/wiki/Onderonian "Onderonian"), having the backing of a Jedi inspired confidence.[[38]](#cite_note-The_Soft_War_Episode_Guide-38) The skills associated with a Jedi Knight were revered and as such, their warrior prowess was known and respected to varies degrees from warrior-like cultures such as [Mandalorians](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian").[[39]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-39) Some outsiders had exaggerated views of the sheer power an average Jedi possessed and attributed them with being able to do things the Jedi themselves considered more to be like divine action.[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24)

However, [anti-Jedi sentiment](/wiki/Anti-Jedi_sentiment "Anti-Jedi sentiment") was also present throughout their history, stronger in some periods than others.[[36]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_3-36) The Sith aimed to purge the galaxy of the Jedi and their ways.[[37]](#cite_note-DB:Order-37) Other groups and factions emerged with anti-Jedi sentiments; various [Mandalorians](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian"), like those of [Death Watch](/wiki/Death_Watch "Death Watch"), held a grudge against the Jedi for their perceived crimes against [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore") during the [Mandalorian-Jedi War](/wiki/Mandalorian-Jedi_War "Mandalorian-Jedi War").[[39]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-39)[[40]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Rebels_Showrunner_Explains_Major_Knight_of_the_Old_Republic_Reference-40) The [Dagoyan Order](/wiki/Dagoyan_Order "Dagoyan Order") also had a chilly relation with up until the later years of the Galactic Republic; early in its history, the Jedi Order had attempted to take in [Bardottan](/wiki/Bardottan "Bardottan") [children](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling"), causing them to cease most contact.[[7]](#cite_note-NoP-7) The [E'roni](/wiki/E%27roni "E'roni") spread stories of the Jedi, with some claiming the Jedi were miracle workers who used the power of levitation and "laser swords." Other E'roni, however, looked down on the Jedi as outsiders. Their rivals, the [Eirami](/wiki/Eirami "Eirami"), did not have stories of the Jedi but spoke of their "[first god](/wiki/Krel_(deity) "Krel (deity)")" in a similar way to how the Jedi described the Force.[[25]](#cite_note-Convergence-25)

A cult known as the [Path of the Open Hand](/wiki/Path_of_the_Open_Hand "Path of the Open Hand") believed the Jedi abused the Force by using it, and thus promoted anti-Jedi sentiment and the belief that the order was the reason for much of the galaxy's suffering. They rose to prominence on the planet [Dalna](/wiki/Dalna "Dalna") during the early [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era"),[[31]](#cite_note-Path_of_Deceit-31) during which time they began to spread their influence and beliefs across the [Dalnan sector](/wiki/Dalnan_sector "Dalnan sector")[[25]](#cite_note-Convergence-25) and the greater galaxy.[[31]](#cite_note-Path_of_Deceit-31) The Path declared that the Force did not belong to the Jedi, which was a claim the Jedi had never actually made.[[25]](#cite_note-Convergence-25)

As the Jedi Order evolved and changed to face the challenges that were current to the galaxy, the way its members acted also had a habit of changing and evolving with time,[[41]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_(2020)_20-41) which often could have an impact on their relationship with the public.[[42]](#cite_note-Dangerous_Debt-42) During the High Republic Era, the Jedi maintained the ideals of avoiding attachment[[33]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-33) but made sure to show great acts of compassion towards those who were suffering, such as offering hugs to those who were grieving.[[43]](#cite_note-THR_3-43) However, many Jedi active in the late Republic Era gave into their need to avoid attachments to a detrimental extent,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) resulting in them instead offering proclamations of the Force and the greater good to those who were grieving, which often left those who were suffering with bitterness and the feeling that the Force users did not truly care.[[42]](#cite_note-Dangerous_Debt-42)

When a Jedi Knight of the High Republic Era had acted in such a way to the young [Axel Greylark](/wiki/Axel_Greylark "Axel Greylark"), as he was forced to leave his [father](/wiki/Lexxir_Greylark "Lexxir Greylark") behind so she could save him and the rest of a starship crew, it generated a lifelong hate for the Jedi in Greylark's heart. Rather than properly comfort the boy, the Jedi Knight had said his father's demise was the will of the Force before moving on with her duties. As he started to grow close to Jedi Knight [Gella Nattai](/wiki/Gella_Nattai "Gella Nattai"), he explained the story to her. While she understood what the Jedi Knight had meant, she knew it would not help Greylark to repeat it and instead affirmed to him that caring for grieving children was important to the Jedi, despite the other Knight's poor word choice.[[25]](#cite_note-Convergence-25) As the Republic Era reached its end, however, the more distant approach won out,[[42]](#cite_note-Dangerous_Debt-42) with many Jedi adopting a more detached persona[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) that, unknowingly, created public dislike towards them.[[42]](#cite_note-Dangerous_Debt-42) Whereas the Jedi of the High Republic did not believe qualities like the age someone came to the Order at or their [midi-chlorian](/wiki/Midi-chlorian "Midi-chlorian") count to be determining factors in whether someone could be a Jedi,[[44]](#cite_note-What_a_Jedi_Makes-44) the later Jedi did overwhelmingly value these factors.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1)

The High Republic Era also saw greater variance in Jedi lightsabers, with differing hilt designs and blade colors seeing greater use[[45]](#cite_note-THR_8-45) when compared to their late Republic counterparts.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_II-5) A shift in lightsaber design culture came during the High Republic Era's Nihil conflict, where the [Guardian Protocols](/wiki/Guardian_Protocols "Guardian Protocols")-minded Jedi Order gave the order to only create simple [battle saber](/wiki/Battle_saber "Battle saber") hilts: if there was to be great conflict, the Council reasoned that lightsabers would be lost and then replaced. As such, the Council ordered Jedi to only create the basic hilt design instead of more unique looks because basic battle sabers were faster to create and maintain in excess.[[46]](#cite_note-Shadows_1-46) The hilts of late Republic lightsaber were largely the same and basic in design,[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_II-5) much like the lightsabers created under the battle saber order.[[46]](#cite_note-Shadows_1-46) All the same, the later period of the High Republic Era had continued to see variance in lightsaber color.[[47]](#cite_note-Trailer-47) The High Republic Jedi also acknowledged a Jedi needed to be more than their lightsaber,[[48]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-48) whereas the late Republic Jedi declared a lightsaber was "[their] life."[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_II-5)

Jedi of the High Republic Era each developed their own understanding of the Force and how to understand it,[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24) with Jedi being allowed to take on the position of "[Wayseeker](/wiki/Wayseeker "Wayseeker")" to avoid the orders of the High Council and follow only the will of the Force. One [Wayseeker](/wiki/Unidentified_Wayseeker "Unidentified Wayseeker") went as far to become an [Alderaanian](/wiki/Alderaanian "Alderaanian") singing sensation.[[49]](#cite_note-Into_the_Dark-49) Beyond establishing temples across the galaxy and working those temples into each planet's culture and environment,[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24) Jedi of the High Republic Era also made a true effort to live amongst the cultures they tried to protect. Instead of simply living in their temples most of the time[[50]](#cite_note-Yoda_interview-50) and only leaving when a mission called,[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_II-5) the Jedi of the High Republic called the galaxy overall their home,[[25]](#cite_note-Convergence-25) establishing new temples[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24) and new missions across the galaxy as they traveled to meet and help the galaxy's cultures.[[25]](#cite_note-Convergence-25)

## History

### Guardians of the Republic

:   "*What was once a simple religious sect devoted to the light side of the Force evolved into the most influential group of peacekeepers in the history of the galaxy.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker, on the Jedi Order[[51]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-51)

 [![The first Jedi Temple was located on Ahch-To, a distant planet in the Unknown Regions of the galaxy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/68/First_Jedi_Temple_TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20180509045418) [![The first Jedi Temple was located on Ahch-To, a distant planet in the Unknown Regions of the galaxy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/68/First_Jedi_Temple_TLJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180509045418)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/68/First_Jedi_Temple_TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20180509045418) 

The first Jedi Temple was located on Ahch-To, a distant planet in the Unknown Regions of the galaxy.

 

The Jedi were an order of ancient origins, having been present in the galaxy for over [one thousand](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium") generations.[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4) Originally established at the [first Jedi Temple](/wiki/First_Jedi_Temple "First Jedi Temple") on [Ahch-To](/wiki/Ahch-To "Ahch-To") by the [Prime Jedi](/wiki/Prime_Jedi "Prime Jedi"),[[6]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-6) the Jedi Order built [temples](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple") and outposts on numerous worlds throughout the galaxy, including [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"), [Ossus](/wiki/Ossus "Ossus"), [Tython](/wiki/Tython "Tython"), and [Jedha](/wiki/Jedha "Jedha"). The Jedi eventually came to align with the [democratic](/wiki/Democracy "Democracy") Galactic Republic and owed their allegiance to the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate").[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) For a time, the Jedi were addressed using the honorary title of "[Lord Jedi](/wiki/Lord_Jedi "Lord Jedi")," but the title fell out of use in the millennium before the High Republic Era, with only the [Togrutas](/wiki/Togruta "Togruta") keeping use of the title.[[52]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-52)

### Wars of the Old Republic

:   "*There have not been battles like these since the days of the Old Republic.*"
:   ―Saesee Tiin[[53]](#cite_note-Citadel_Rescue-53)

 [![The Sith splintered from the Jedi to follow the dark side, spawning a rivalry that lasted for millennia.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/JediVsSith-SOTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20220502004842) [![The Sith splintered from the Jedi to follow the dark side, spawning a rivalry that lasted for millennia.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/JediVsSith-SOTS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20220502004842)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a5/JediVsSith-SOTS.png/revision/latest?cb=20220502004842) 

The Sith splintered from the Jedi to follow the dark side, spawning a rivalry that lasted for millennia.

 

When a [rogue Jedi](/wiki/Unidentified_rogue_Jedi "Unidentified rogue Jedi") was [exiled](/wiki/Exile_(punishment) "Exile (punishment)") from the order after advocating the use of the dark side of the Force, they gained followers which led to the creation of the Sith[[54]](#cite_note-Sith-54) during the [Hundred-Year Darkness](/wiki/Hundred-Year_Darkness "Hundred-Year Darkness").[[55]](#cite_note-Showdown_on_the_Smuggler's_Moon,_Part_II-55) The Jedi and Sith became bitter enemies,[[56]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-56) engaging in a number of battles and wars like the [Sith war](/wiki/Sith_war_(Old_Republic) "Sith war (Old Republic)"),[[7]](#cite_note-NoP-7) the [Battle of Takodana](/wiki/Battle_of_Takodana_(Jedi_versus_Sith) "Battle of Takodana (Jedi versus Sith)"),[[57]](#cite_note-TVD-57) the [Great Hyperspace War](/wiki/Great_Hyperspace_War "Great Hyperspace War"),[[7]](#cite_note-NoP-7) the [Great Sith War](/wiki/Great_Sith_War "Great Sith War"),[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24) the [Great Scourge of Malachor](/wiki/Great_Scourge_of_Malachor "Great Scourge of Malachor"),[[58]](#cite_note-Twilight_of_the_Apprentice-58) the [resurgence of the Sith](/wiki/Resurgence_of_the_Sith "Resurgence of the Sith"),[[59]](#cite_note-KoF-59) and [the defeat](/wiki/Darth_Momin%27s_destruction_of_a_city "Darth Momin's destruction of a city") of [Darth Momin](/wiki/Darth_Momin "Darth Momin").[[60]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_22-60)

Another splinter group of Jedi emerged, calling themselves the [Ordu Aspectu](/wiki/Ordu_Aspectu "Ordu Aspectu"). Some records suggested they had hoped to give [immortality](/wiki/Immortality "Immortality") to everyone in the galaxy, yet others believed that they may have killed Jedi [Padawans](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") to try to achieve their goals.[[8]](#cite_note-Doctor_Aphra_2-8) The Ordu Aspectu and the "orthodox" Jedi[[61]](#cite_note-Doctor_Aphra_5-61) came to fight against each other in the [Entruvia Conflict](/wiki/Entruvia_Conflict "Entruvia Conflict"), which ended with a [peace treaty](/wiki/Jedi%E2%80%93Ordu_Aspectu_treaty "Jedi–Ordu Aspectu treaty"). The treaty allowed the Ordu to continue their research into immortality, but gave the Jedi Order the right to inspect the research. The [doom of the Ordu Aspectu](/wiki/Attack_on_Garn "Attack on Garn"), however, would result in the destruction of the splinter order and the Jedi inspectors: the leader of the Aspectu—a man named [Rur](/wiki/Rur "Rur")—was able to download his mind into a computer, creating the [Eternal Rur](/wiki/Eternal_Rur "Eternal Rur"), which wiped out everyone present.[[62]](#cite_note-Doctor_Aphra_6-62) At another point in the Jedi Order's history, in the aftermath of the [Corsair Wars](/wiki/Corsair_Wars "Corsair Wars"), Jedi Master [Oo'ob](/wiki/Oo%27ob "Oo'ob") broke from doctrine to create the [Farkiller](/wiki/Farkiller "Farkiller").[[63]](#cite_note-Aphra_33-63)

The [Great Jedi Library](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Library "Great Jedi Library") on Ossus was destroyed at some point prior to the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars").[[3]](#cite_note-CL-3) At some point before the construction of the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") on the planet Coruscant, the Jedi [evacuated](/wiki/Evacuation_of_Ossus "Evacuation of Ossus") a few of the [holobooks](/wiki/Holobook "Holobook") and artifacts from the lost Great Library which made it to the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives "Jedi Archives") on Coruscant.[[7]](#cite_note-NoP-7) At some point, the mosaic floor of the [First Temple](/wiki/First_Temple "First Temple") on Ossus was salvaged and transported to the Order's newer headquarters on Coruscant.[[3]](#cite_note-CL-3) In the quasi-historical [Qel-Droma Epics](/wiki/Qel-Droma_Epics "Qel-Droma Epics"), Ossus was decimated during the [Cron Supernova](/wiki/Cron_Supernova "Cron Supernova")[[7]](#cite_note-NoP-7) around [4000 BBY](/wiki/4,000_BBY "4,000 BBY"),[[64]](#cite_note-Supernova_Date-64) when the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Naga Sadow](/wiki/Naga_Sadow "Naga Sadow") triggered [stars](/wiki/Star "Star") in the [Cron Cluster](/wiki/Cron_Cluster "Cron Cluster") to become [supernovae](/wiki/Supernova "Supernova"). The Jedi had little warning of the coming cataclysm and prioritized the artifacts from the [Chamber of Antiquities](/wiki/Chamber_of_Antiquities "Chamber of Antiquities") of the Great Jedi Library. Despite the efforts, they only managed to save a fraction of the artifacts housed on the planet, which made it to the Jedi Temple on the planet Coruscant via nearby [Exis Station](/wiki/Exis_Station "Exis Station"), leaving the Great Library in ruins.[[7]](#cite_note-NoP-7)

Also during the reign of the Old Republic, the Mandalorians, the [warrior people](/wiki/Mandalorian_warrior "Mandalorian warrior") of the planet Mandalore, launched a number of wars, often coming into conflict with the Jedi.[[65]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-65) Battles between the Mandalorians and Jedi dated back to the time of the [Mandalorian crusaders](/wiki/Mandalorian_crusaders "Mandalorian crusaders").[[66]](#cite_note-Shades_Trivia_Gallery-66) According to legend, [Mandalore the Great](/wiki/Mandalore_the_Great "Mandalore the Great") led the Mandalorians against the Jedi in a number of battles.[[67]](#cite_note-Chapter_8-67) Eventually, the Mandalorians developed [their distinctive armor](/wiki/Mandalorian_armor "Mandalorian armor")[[68]](#cite_note-Chapter_1-68) in order to combat their [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") enemies.[[28]](#cite_note-Complete_Visual_New-28)

 [![The world of Mandalore was devastated in the conflict between the Mandalorians and the Jedi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/Mandalore_mural.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250926050127) [![The world of Mandalore was devastated in the conflict between the Mandalorians and the Jedi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/Mandalore_mural.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250926050127)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/Mandalore_mural.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250926050127) 

The world of Mandalore was devastated in the conflict between the Mandalorians and the Jedi.

 

The war against the Mandalorians ended in a decisive Jedi victory.[[69]](#cite_note-Trials_of_the_Darksaber-69) In the process, the surface of Mandalore was devastated[[70]](#cite_note-Creating_Mandalore-70) during [the final battle](/wiki/Annihilation "Annihilation") between Mandalorian [warlords](/wiki/Warlord "Warlord")[[71]](#cite_note-Mandalorian_super_commando-71) and the Jedi Order.[[70]](#cite_note-Creating_Mandalore-70) Also at some point, as recounted in legend, a Force-sensitive Mandalorian named [Tarre Vizsla](/wiki/Tarre_Vizsla "Tarre Vizsla") was inducted into the Jedi Order. His lightsaber, the [Darksaber](/wiki/Darksaber "Darksaber"), was stored in the Jedi Temple on Coruscant after his death until members of [House Vizsla](/wiki/House_Vizsla "House Vizsla") [broke in and stole the blade](/wiki/Sacking_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Sacking of the Jedi Temple")[[69]](#cite_note-Trials_of_the_Darksaber-69) during the [fall of the Old Republic](/wiki/Fall_of_the_Old_Republic "Fall of the Old Republic"). The Darksaber went on to be used to cut down many Jedi[[65]](#cite_note-The_Mandalore_Plot-65) and unite the Mandalorian people as a symbol of leadership.[[69]](#cite_note-Trials_of_the_Darksaber-69)

The Old Republic crumbled as a result of the Jedi-Sith wars, but its remnants and the Jedi still waged the [final war](/wiki/Jedi-Sith_War "Jedi-Sith War") against the Sith.[[72]](#cite_note-SWP-72) Ultimately, the Sith's greed for power caused them to turn on each other, which helped the Jedi [defeat and decimate](/wiki/Defeat_of_the_Sith "Defeat of the Sith") the weakened Sith. However, one [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord"), [Darth Bane](/wiki/Darth_Bane "Darth Bane"), secretly survived the destruction and continued the Sith by creating the [Rule of Two](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two")[[56]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-56) and initiating the [Great Plan](/wiki/Grand_Plan "Grand Plan").[[73]](#cite_note-HC_2-73) The Jedi would discover and then think they destroyed Bane's rule,[[74]](#cite_note-SW_2020_20-74) but the Sith continued to survive in secret under the Rule of Two.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1)

### The Great Peace

#### Jedi of the Republic

##### Across the galaxy

 [![The Jedi reached the pinnacle of their power and influence during the height of the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/PaoloVillanelliTHR1Virgin.png/revision/latest?cb=20210307014711) [![The Jedi reached the pinnacle of their power and influence during the height of the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/PaoloVillanelliTHR1Virgin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20210307014711)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/PaoloVillanelliTHR1Virgin.png/revision/latest?cb=20210307014711) 

The Jedi reached the pinnacle of their power and influence during the height of the Galactic Republic.

 

After the defeat and assumed destruction of the Sith, the Jedi Order enjoyed a political ascension and saw an increase in recruitment. During the so-called "[Great Peace](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era")" enjoyed by the Galactic Republic,[[75]](#cite_note-Rise-75) which had reinvented itself after the defeat of the Sith,[[72]](#cite_note-SWP-72) the Jedi maintained a reputation[[76]](#cite_note-VoT-76) and role of being peacekeepers despite their limited numbers.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_II-5) The Jedi took part in[[77]](#cite_note-2022_THR_1-77) the [Republic-Togruta conflict](/wiki/Republic-Togruta_conflict "Republic-Togruta conflict").[[52]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-52) The [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era") in particular was the height of the Jedi Order's power,[[78]](#cite_note-Light_dust_jacket-78) being a time of greatly expanded Jedi activity throughout the galaxy that even allowed them to stretch out far from the [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds").[[79]](#cite_note-Kylo_2-79) During the era, the Jedi worked closely with the Republic.[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24) In the days of the [Great Hyperspace Rush](/wiki/Great_Hyperspace_Rush "Great Hyperspace Rush"), the Jedi worked with [Outer Rim Exploration Teams](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Exploration_Team "Outer Rim Exploration Team") sent out by Supreme Chancellors [Orlen Mollo](/wiki/Orlen_Mollo "Orlen Mollo") and [Kyong Greylark](/wiki/Kyong_Greylark "Kyong Greylark"), who both hoped to unite the galaxy. Even Jedi who were not currently working with [Republic Pathfinders](/wiki/Republic_Pathfinder "Republic Pathfinder") were expected to perform similar work, introducing themselves to and learning from local cultures, as well as looking for possible temple locations and Force-sensitive children. The Jedi hoped to prove themselves to the people of the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories") as defenders they could rely on.[[31]](#cite_note-Path_of_Deceit-31)

However, the Republic and Jedi's expansion into the Outer Rim brought them into conflict with the Path of the Open Hand cult, which believed the Jedi were actively hurting the galaxy by using the Force. As part of their campaign to root out the supposed abusers of the Force, the Path unleashed[[31]](#cite_note-Path_of_Deceit-31) a [Nameless](/wiki/Shrikarai "Shrikarai")[[80]](#cite_note-Trail_of_Shadows_5-80) later known as the [Great Leveler](/wiki/Great_Leveler "Great Leveler"), which feasted upon Force users.[[52]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-52) Jedi [Sav Malagán](/wiki/Savina_Besatrix_Malag%C3%A1n "Savina Besatrix Malagán") fought alongside a pirate crew led by [Maz Kanata](/wiki/Maz_Kanata "Maz Kanata") during the [Battle of Jedha](/wiki/Battle_of_Jedha "Battle of Jedha").[[81]](#cite_note-HRA_9-81) The defeat of the Path would come with the [Night of Sorrow](/wiki/Night_of_Sorrow "Night of Sorrow"), during which the Path unleashed a number of Nameless against the Jedi. After the battle, Yoda and Jedi Master [Creighton Sun](/wiki/Creighton_Sun "Creighton Sun") decided to cover up the existence of the Nameless until more could be learned about the mysterious threat, reasoning that details about the beings getting out would be a danger to the Order. However, the decision[[48]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-48) left later Jedi vulnerable to an enemy they were not prepared for.[[80]](#cite_note-Trail_of_Shadows_5-80) Victory over the Path was seen as proof of how well the Jedi-Republic partnership worked out for the galaxy.[[48]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-48) However, later in the High Republic Era, some Jedi, such as Master [Cohmac Vitus](/wiki/Cohmac_Vitus "Cohmac Vitus"), came to question whether it was right for the Jedi to work so closely with the Republic. In particular, Vitus pointed to the Night of Sorrow as a tragic event that had come about due to a joint Republic-Jedi effort.[[82]](#cite_note-Out_of_the_Shadows-82)

Nevertheless, with the Republic seeking to bring the Outer Rim into its domain through projects like [Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Starlight_Beacon "Starlight Beacon"), the Order agreed to establish outposts in the Outer Rim, establishing these outposts to provide help to people in the galaxy's wilder locations and to help explore these places. Prior to the [dedication of Starlight](/wiki/Dedication_of_the_Starlight_Beacon "Dedication of the Starlight Beacon"), these outposts and their three to seven Jedi occupants—operating separately from the Jedi Temple on Coruscant—became the only force for justice on the [Galactic Frontier](/wiki/Galactic_Frontier "Galactic Frontier").[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24) During the High Republic, the foremost Jedi Master of the era, [Avar Kriss](/wiki/Avar_Kriss "Avar Kriss"),[[83]](#cite_note-Databank_Avar-83) held a rare Force power amongst the Jedi; able to detect the natural [Force-bonds](/wiki/Force-bond "Force-bond") among Force-sensitives, she could strengthen them into a [network](/wiki/Song_of_the_Force "Song of the Force") of many Jedi. She was also close with Knight [Elzar Mann](/wiki/Elzar_Mann "Elzar Mann"), whose experiments through trying different Force techniques helped expand the Order's knowledge of the energy field. Under the leadership of Kriss, Mann and her were among the hundred Jedi dispatched to the [Hetzal system](/wiki/Hetzal_system "Hetzal system") in response to the sudden [Great Hyperspace Disaster](/wiki/Great_Hyperspace_Disaster "Great Hyperspace Disaster"), which began when fragments of the transport *[Legacy Run](/wiki/Legacy_Run "Legacy Run")* began to fall upon the star system thanks to the machinations of the [Eye of the Nihil](/wiki/Eye_of_the_Nihil "Eye of the Nihil") [Marchion Ro](/wiki/Marchion_Ro "Marchion Ro"), whose [family](/wiki/Ro_family "Ro family") had a history with the Jedi:[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24) their ancestors, [Yana Ro](/wiki/Yana_Ro "Yana Ro") and [Marda Ro](/wiki/Marda_Ro "Marda Ro"), had been part of the Path of the Open Hand.[[31]](#cite_note-Path_of_Deceit-31) The Ro family would later remember "the faithful" as waging war with the Jedi because of their differing belief systems, believing the Jedi were unable to fulfill "balance" and were leading the galaxy to death.[[52]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-52)

To Marchion himself, the Jedi were not merely dangerous because they could use the Force; he believed their united Order gave them a structure to rely on, confidence, and a willingness to make large scale decisions, all in the name of spreading their light. Faced with an enemy who were therefore bold and strong, Ro, while not afraid of the Jedi, understood they would be a serious threat to his goals, which involved wiping them out. With Kriss using her network to inform her fellow Force-sensitives that the fragments contained living beings, the Jedi led the [Republic Defense Coalition](/wiki/Republic_Defense_Coalition "Republic Defense Coalition") to rescue the star system and those trapped aboard the starship remains before turning their combined attention towards a fragment containing liquid [Tibanna](/wiki/Tibanna "Tibanna"). Despite the failure of their first attempt and the loss of several Jedi, the Force users—joined in focus by Jedi in other locations in the galaxy—ultimately ensured the fragment did not collide with an [R-class](/wiki/R-class "R-class") [sun](/wiki/Star "Star"), saving the system. Additionally, the effort was broadcasted to various other worlds; only those who hated the Jedi were angered by their success.[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24)

##### Conflict with the Nihil

 [![The peace of the Republic, maintained by the Jedi, was disrupted by the Emergences and the Nihil conflict.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/THR-TheFallenStar-OOP-FullArt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220105191453) [![The peace of the Republic, maintained by the Jedi, was disrupted by the Emergences and the Nihil conflict.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/THR-TheFallenStar-OOP-FullArt.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220105191453)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/THR-TheFallenStar-OOP-FullArt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220105191453) 

The peace of the Republic, maintained by the Jedi, was disrupted by the Emergences and the Nihil conflict.

 

As the galaxy was faced with the [Emergences](/wiki/Emergences "Emergences"), forcing the Republic to [blockade](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade") a growing number of [hyperspace routes](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route") into the Outer Rim, the Jedi Council believed the Jedi were going to be heavily needed in the region. Additionally, [Nihil](/wiki/Nihil "Nihil") became known, leading to [conflict between the pirates and the Jedi](/wiki/Nihil_conflict "Nihil conflict"). Jedi Master [Loden Greatstorm](/wiki/Loden_Greatstorm "Loden Greatstorm") was captured by the Nihil during the [raid on Elphrona](/wiki/Raid_on_Elphrona "Raid on Elphrona"), playing into Ro's plans.[[24]](#cite_note-Light_of_the_Jedi-24) During the Nihil conflict, the Republic began to push the Jedi to more closely work alongside them, with [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Lina Soh](/wiki/Lina_Soh "Lina Soh") and her [aides](/wiki/Aide "Aide") moving to insert themselves into the Jedi Council's affairs.[[82]](#cite_note-Out_of_the_Shadows-82) Torturing Greatstorm for a year, Ro also came to collect all pieces to a [family artifact](/wiki/Nameless_control_rods "Nameless control rods") he could use to unleash the Great Leveler. After the [massive Nihil raid](/wiki/Valo_Atrocity "Valo Atrocity") on the [Valo Republic Fair](/wiki/Valo_Republic_Fair "Valo Republic Fair"), the Jedi tracked the Nihil to the planet [Grizal](/wiki/Grizal "Grizal"), only for Ro to unleash the Leveler during the [enusing battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Grizal "Battle of Grizal"); Greatstorm was killed, with his body left to turn to stone that soon crumbled, [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Bell Zettifar](/wiki/Bell_Zettifar "Bell Zettifar") and Jedi Master Elzar Mann were left in states of shock, and Council member [Stellan Gios](/wiki/Stellan_Gios "Stellan Gios") was left to feel afraid.[[52]](#cite_note-The_Rising_Storm-52)

Ro struck a further blow to the Jedi and Republic with the [destruction of Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Destruction_of_Starlight_Beacon "Destruction of Starlight Beacon"), during which he deployed more Nameless. Unable to fight the creatures, the Jedi Order recalled all its members to Coruscant to strategize, only for Ro to [claim](/wiki/Deployment_of_the_stormseeds "Deployment of the stormseeds") a portion of the Outer Rim as [Nihil space](/wiki/Occlusion_Zone "Occlusion Zone").[[84]](#cite_note-Eye_2-84) Eventually, the Nihil were destroyed.[[85]](#cite_note-SW7-85)

##### Continued "Great Peace" era

:   "*I remember a time when Jedi were not generals, but peacekeepers.*"
:   ―Satine Kryze — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b7/NotGeneralsButPeacekeepers.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250328195708)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:NotGeneralsButPeacekeepers.flac "File:NotGeneralsButPeacekeepers.flac"))[[76]](#cite_note-VoT-76)

As time went by, the Jedi continued to be involved in a number of the conflicts that [sectors](/wiki/Sector "Sector") and [planets](/wiki/Planet "Planet") faced throughout the so-called "Great Peace." Though these conflicts could at times force them to act as military officers,[[75]](#cite_note-Rise-75) the Jedi did not view themselves as soldiers.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_II-5) The Jedi would also work as warriors, troubleshooters, and [diplomats](/wiki/Diplomat "Diplomat") for the Republic but claimed to be impartial judges. However, given that they were working for the Republic, trust in the Jedi was not the same for everyone. The citizens closer to the Core Worlds trusted them more than those in the Outer Rim Territories.[[75]](#cite_note-Rise-75) The Jedi became involved in conflicts like the [Mandalorian Civil War](/wiki/Great_Clan_Wars "Great Clan Wars"),[[76]](#cite_note-VoT-76) the [battle for Ontotho](/wiki/Battle_for_Ontotho "Battle for Ontotho"),[[86]](#cite_note-Jedi_5-86) and the [Stark Hyperspace War](/wiki/Stark_Hyperspace_War "Stark Hyperspace War").[[87]](#cite_note-Force_Collection-87)

#### Return of the Sith

:   "*Rage… it fuels us. But it won't be enough to stop the Jedi alone. They have numbers on their side. And the faith of the Republic.*"  
    "*For the moment. In time, and with careful planning, they will lose both.*"
:   ―Darth Maul and Darth Sidious[[88]](#cite_note-Age_Maul-88)

 [![For generations the Sith plotted revenge on the Jedi for the defeat of their forebears.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3f/Malachor-AORDarthMaul1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190413150654) [![For generations the Sith plotted revenge on the Jedi for the defeat of their forebears.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3f/Malachor-AORDarthMaul1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190413150654)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3f/Malachor-AORDarthMaul1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190413150654) 

For generations the Sith plotted revenge on the Jedi for the defeat of their forebears.

 

Although the Jedi believed their sworn enemies to be extinct, the Sith had survived under the Rule of Two, influencing the galaxy from the shadows instead of battlefields. After around a thousand years of [Sith Masters](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master") and [Sith apprentices](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice"),[[75]](#cite_note-Rise-75) the Sith Lord who held the rank of Master was [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"),[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) a [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo_(people) "Naboo (people)") who had been trained by the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") [Darth Plagueis](/wiki/Darth_Plagueis "Darth Plagueis").[[89]](#cite_note-USW-89) After betraying Plagueis by killing him in his sleep, Sidious sought to accomplish the Sith plan to bring the galaxy under his control as its [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor").[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) Sidious also had his own Sith apprentice, [Darth Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul"). Due to his desire to kill Jedi, Maul killed Padawan [Eldra Kaitis](/wiki/Eldra_Kaitis "Eldra Kaitis") on the [moon of Drazkel](/wiki/Moon_of_Drazkel "Moon of Drazkel"), but her death did not satisfy his bloodlust.[[90]](#cite_note-Darth_Maul_5-90) Thus, establishing a fake [cartel](/wiki/Kaitis_Cartel "Kaitis Cartel") under Kaitis's name, Maul continued his hunt and killed the Force-sensitive [thief](/wiki/Thief "Thief") [Zek Peiro](/wiki/Zek_Peiro "Zek Peiro"). Not wanting the Jedi to learn of his plans, Sidious brought Maul to[[88]](#cite_note-Age_Maul-88) the ancient Sith world[[58]](#cite_note-Twilight_of_the_Apprentice-58) of [Malachor](/wiki/Malachor "Malachor") to teach him about patience. Maul experienced a [Force vision](/wiki/Force_vision "Force vision") of a life where he was a Jedi before being surrounded by dozens of them, teaching him that their light side rivals had numbers and the respect of the Republic for the time being.[[88]](#cite_note-Age_Maul-88)

Sidious' public identity was Sheev Palpatine, the [senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") of his [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo"). Living a double life allowed him to pursue political power in the Senate while conspiring to overthrow the Republic and its Jedi protectors as Sidious.[[91]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-91) He planned to become [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") of the Republic to bring about his rule, so he ordered his pawns in the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation") to [blockade](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") his own home planet[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1) to generate sympathy in the Senate[[92]](#cite_note-On_the_Front_Lines-92) and make Supreme Chancellor [Finis Valorum](/wiki/Finis_Valorum "Finis Valorum") look weak.[[93]](#cite_note-Sidious_BioGal2-93) When Valorum sent two [ambassadors](/wiki/Ambassador "Ambassador"), Jedi Master Qui-Gon Jinn and Padawan [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"), to negotiate an end to the blockade, Sidious ordered them killed, but the two Jedi [escaped](/wiki/Escape_from_the_Saak%27ak "Escape from the Saak'ak") to Naboo's surface and [rescued](/wiki/Capture_of_Theed "Capture of Theed") [Queen](/wiki/Monarch_of_Naboo "Monarch of Naboo") [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") and her entourage.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1)

Due to the damage sustained during their escape, the [Naboo Royal Starship](/wiki/Naboo_Royal_Starship "Naboo Royal Starship") needed to land on the [desert](/wiki/Desert "Desert") planet of [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine"). On Tatooine, Jinn met Anakin Skywalker, a young Force-sensitive human who he came to believe was the Chosen One. In fact, thanks to his power in the Force, Skywalker won the [Boonta Eve Classic](/wiki/Boonta_Eve_Classic "Boonta Eve Classic"), which won him freedom from his slavery under [Watto](/wiki/Watto "Watto") the [junk dealer](/wiki/Junk_dealer "Junk dealer"), albeit without freeing his mother, [Shmi](/wiki/Shmi_Skywalker_Lars "Shmi Skywalker Lars"), and a new [T-14 hyperdrive generator](/wiki/T-14_hyperdrive_generator "T-14 hyperdrive generator") for the Royal Starship. Before leaving the planet, Jinn was suddenly [attacked](/wiki/Duel_on_Tatooine "Duel on Tatooine") by Maul, who had been sent to Tatooine by Sidious. Jinn escaped, marking the first time a Jedi had contact with a Sith[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1) and survived to warn the Order[[90]](#cite_note-Darth_Maul_5-90) in a thousand years.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1)

 [![During the Invasion of Naboo, the Jedi learned of the Sith's survival and the existence of the Chosen One.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/Jedi_Council_EP_I.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190110205923) [![During the Invasion of Naboo, the Jedi learned of the Sith's survival and the existence of the Chosen One.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/Jedi_Council_EP_I.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190110205923)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/Jedi_Council_EP_I.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190110205923) 

During the Invasion of Naboo, the Jedi learned of the Sith's survival and the existence of the Chosen One.

 

On the Republic capital of Coruscant, the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") were disturbed by the potential return of the Sith and unwilling to begin Skywalker's training, citing his fear and believing it could lead to the dark side. They then dispatched Jinn and Kenobi back to Naboo when Amidala chose to return, as she had only managed to call for an [election](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor_election,_32_BBY "Supreme Chancellor election, 32 BBY") after being deceived by Palpatine, which would soon lead to Palpatine's victory. During the ensuing [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo"), Jinn and Kenobi engaged Maul in yet another duel, while Skywalker, joined by [astromech droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid") [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2"), joined the space battle against the [*Lucrehulk*-class Battleship](/wiki/Lucrehulk-class_battleship "Lucrehulk-class battleship") *[Vuutun Palaa](/wiki/Vuutun_Palaa "Vuutun Palaa")* in a [N-1 starfighter](/wiki/N-1_starfighter "N-1 starfighter"). Skywalker eventually crashed aboard the [warship](/wiki/Warship "Warship") and, in an attempt to take out advancing [OOM-series security droids](/wiki/OOM-series_security_droid "OOM-series security droid"), fired two [proton torpedoes](/wiki/Proton_torpedo "Proton torpedo") that instead collided with a [reactor](/wiki/Reactor "Reactor"). The ensuing explosion rippled throughout the [battleship](/wiki/Battleship "Battleship"), destroying the craft and therefore shutting down the entire [Trade Federation Droid Army](/wiki/Trade_Federation_Droid_Army "Trade Federation Droid Army") below.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1)

Elsewhere, Maul managed to kill Jinn while he was separated from Kenobi, though the Padawan then engaged Maul and cut the Sith Lord in half, ending the duel. In his dying breaths, Jinn asked Kenobi to train Skywalker, which the Jedi Council agreed to. Additionally, at the [funeral of Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Funeral_of_Qui-Gon_Jinn "Funeral of Qui-Gon Jinn"), Jedi Masters Yoda and [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") spoke about the Sith, unsure whether it was the Sith Master or Sith apprentice who had been defeated.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1) Kenobi was promoted to be a Jedi Knight with Skywalker as his Padawan.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_II-5) Though presumed dead, Maul had survived the duel. Sustained by his newfound hatred of Kenobi,[[94]](#cite_note-Revenge-94) he was left in exile on the garbage world of [Lotho Minor](/wiki/Lotho_Minor "Lotho Minor") for years to come.[[95]](#cite_note-Brothers-95)

### Fall of the Republic

#### The Clone Wars

:   "*I am sure you are aware that the Jedi did not initiate the Clone Wars. Our only intention is to end it and restore peace to our galaxy.*"  
    "*What difference does it make who started the war, and who only wants to end it? No side is free of fault. It takes two to fight.*"  
    "*But isn't liberty worth fighting for?*"  
    "*But is it worth killing for? Fighting for something doesn't necessarily mean that you have to destroy everything in your path. Only when you lay your arms down and pursue a course of non-violence, can you make this claim to me that the Jedi are peacekeepers.*"
:   ―[Aayla Secura](/wiki/Aayla_Secura "Aayla Secura") and [Tee Watt Kaa](/wiki/Tee_Watt_Kaa "Tee Watt Kaa")[[96]](#cite_note-Jedi_Crash-96)

 [![The Jedi were too few in number to protect the Republic against an army of battle droids.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/JediGeonosisArena.png/revision/latest?cb=20200628201303) [![The Jedi were too few in number to protect the Republic against an army of battle droids.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/JediGeonosisArena.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200628201303)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/JediGeonosisArena.png/revision/latest?cb=20200628201303) 

The Jedi were too few in number to protect the Republic against an army of battle droids.

 

From [24 BBY](/wiki/24_BBY "24 BBY")[[97]](#cite_note-24_BBY_date-97) to [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY"),[[10]](#cite_note-Timelines-10) the galaxy was faced with the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis"), a plot manufactured by the Sith. Several thousand [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") sought to secede to the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"), a breakaway government led by its [Head of State](/wiki/Head_of_State "Head of State"), [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), the latter of whom was following Sidious's command. The political tensions boiled into a full-scale war on [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis"), where the Separatist-aligned [Geonosians](/wiki/Geonosian "Geonosian") [sentenced](/wiki/Death_penalty "Death penalty") Kenobi, Skywalker, and the now-[Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") Amidala to death. They were rescued by the arrival of a [Jedi assault team](/wiki/Jedi_assault_team "Jedi assault team") led by Windu and then a force of [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper"), an army of [cloned](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") soldiers recently discovered by Kenobi on the planet [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino"), led by Yoda. In the subsequent actions of the [Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis"), the Jedi led the clones into battle against the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army"), but Dooku managed to escape from Kenobi, Skywalker, and Yoda. Thus, the battle had served to launch the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), the first pan-galactic war[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_II-5) since the alleged extinction of the Sith.[[75]](#cite_note-Rise-75) The start of the war shook the balance of the Force.[[98]](#cite_note-Battle_of_GeoTrailer-98) Dooku informed his master that the war had begun, which satisfied Sidious, who said everything was going as planned.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9)

 [![The Jedi served as generals of the Grand Army of the Republic throughout the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Assault_on_Mandalorian_supply_outpost.png/revision/latest?cb=20140716203005) [![The Jedi served as generals of the Grand Army of the Republic throughout the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Assault_on_Mandalorian_supply_outpost.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140716203005)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Assault_on_Mandalorian_supply_outpost.png/revision/latest?cb=20140716203005) 

The Jedi served as generals of the Grand Army of the Republic throughout the Clone Wars.

 

There were ten thousand Jedi in the galaxy before the Clone Wars,[[99]](#cite_note-Path_of_the_Jedi-99) but many were killed during the conflict,[[100]](#cite_note-Assassin-100) with one Separatist leader, [General](/wiki/General "General") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous"), even being a [Jedi hunter](/wiki/Jedi_hunter "Jedi hunter")[[101]](#cite_note-Databank_Grievous-101) who took the lightsabers of his victims as trophies.[[102]](#cite_note-Lair_of_Grievous-102) Another one of Dooku's agents was the [Dark Acolyte](/wiki/Dark_Acolyte "Dark Acolyte") [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress "Asajj Ventress"), who had been a Padawan to Jedi Knight [Ky Narec](/wiki/Ky_Narec "Ky Narec") in the years before the Clone Wars.[[103]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-103) During the war, Jedi Knights and Masters became the [Jedi Generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") in the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic"), while their Padawans became lower ranking [Jedi Commanders](/wiki/Jedi_Commander "Jedi Commander").[[104]](#cite_note-Clone_Wars_film-104) The war against the Separatists was fought across the galaxy for three years,[[105]](#cite_note-Catalyst-105) during which the Jedi inspired creative thinking and independence in the clones.[[106]](#cite_note-TCW|Fugitive-106) Jedi like [Plo Koon](/wiki/Plo_Koon "Plo Koon"),[[107]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-107) Kenobi,[[108]](#cite_note-Battle_Tales_5-108) Yoda,[[109]](#cite_note-Ambush-109) and Skywalker respected the clones as individuals.[[110]](#cite_note-Darkness-110)

 [![Anakin Skywalker was considered the greatest warrior the Jedi had during the war, becoming known as the "Hero With No Fear".](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Felucia-Skywalker.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100508011908) [![Anakin Skywalker was considered the greatest warrior the Jedi had during the war, becoming known as the "Hero With No Fear".](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Felucia-Skywalker.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20100508011908)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Felucia-Skywalker.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100508011908) 

Anakin Skywalker was considered the greatest warrior the Jedi had during the war, becoming known as the "Hero With No Fear".

 

By fighting the Clone Wars, the Jedi, particularly younger members of the Order, ran the risk of losing their way by focusing on power to win.[[102]](#cite_note-Lair_of_Grievous-102) Their new role as battlefield generals also made some people cast doubt on their role as "peacekeepers,"[[76]](#cite_note-VoT-76)[[96]](#cite_note-Jedi_Crash-96) with one Padawan, [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee "Barriss Offee"), and other Republic citizens even coming to view the Jedi to be responsible for the war. Falling to the dark side and thinking her Order had fallen from the light to be an army that only benefitted the dark side, Offee arranged for a [bombing of the Jedi Temple hangar](/wiki/Bombing_of_the_Jedi_Temple_hangar "Bombing of the Jedi Temple hangar") and framed her friend, fellow Padawan [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano"), to take the fall. One of the few people to stand with Tano was Skywalker, who was Tano's master and friend. He uncovered and exposed Offee as the true culprit during [Tano's trial](/wiki/Trial_of_Ahsoka_Tano "Trial of Ahsoka Tano"). Nevertheless, with her faith in the Order shaken, Tano left the Jedi to go on her own path,[[111]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-111) but she remained on the light side and acted, according to [Rafa Martez](/wiki/Rafa_Martez "Rafa Martez"), in the way the Jedi should have been.[[112]](#cite_note-Together_Again-112) Meanwhile, Skywalker greatly missed his Padawan[[113]](#cite_note-In_Search_of_the_Crystal-113) and was frustrated with the Jedi Council, feeling they had betrayed his friend.[[114]](#cite_note-backstories-114) During the war, Skywalker gained prominence and recognition for his victories on the battlefield, being considered the greatest warrior of the Jedi Order during the Clone Wars.[[115]](#cite_note-Shroud_of_Darkness-115)

#### The End of the Jedi

:   "*The Jedi were* good*. Like all of us, they failed to secure the peace. They were drawn into the war like everyone else, and their hands were* not *clean. If I can accept the blame for my part, they certainly earned their share, too.* But *for thousands of years they could have ruled the galaxy, and instead they chose to serve. They had their own vested interests, their own ways of politicking. But they believed their power came with an obligation to live humbly, to do good without asserting authority. Maybe they failed to live up to those ideals in the end. I haven't seen your evidence. What do* I *know about the extent of their betrayals? But they were good and they were ordinary and they were fallible, and even the most smug and arrogant were trying to hew to a tradition older than the Republic. They deserved better than to die at the hands of power-hungry old men who saw them as a threat.* We *deserved better than to lose another people, another religion, from the universe. All of us are poorer for their loss.* […] *The Jedi deserve justice… or at least a decent funeral.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma, to Soujen Vak-Nhalis[[116]](#cite_note-MoF-116)

 [![Having learned that the Supreme Chancellor was a Sith Lord, the Jedi moved to arrest Darth Sidious before his plans came to fruition.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111028234030) [![Having learned that the Supreme Chancellor was a Sith Lord, the Jedi moved to arrest Darth Sidious before his plans came to fruition.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111028234030)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111028234030) 

Having learned that the Supreme Chancellor was a Sith Lord, the Jedi moved to arrest Darth Sidious before his plans came to fruition.

 

In the [Battle of Coruscant](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant"), which was staged by Sidious, in order to lure Anakin to the dark side and eventually make the young Jedi his apprentice, Dooku was betrayed by his master who had him killed by Skywalker. Following the battle, Skywalker had visions of Amidala, who he had [secretly married](/wiki/Wedding_of_Anakin_Skywalker_and_Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Wedding of Anakin Skywalker and Padmé Amidala"), dying in childbirth. Shortly thereafter, Palpatine, who had long since befriended Skywalker to manipulate him, informed the Jedi Knight that he was in fact Darth Sidious, the Sith Master behind the war and the target the Jedi had been searching for. After Skywalker informed Windu of Palpatine's identity and deception, the Jedi Master led [Kit Fisto](/wiki/Kit_Fisto "Kit Fisto"), [Agen Kolar](/wiki/Agen_Kolar "Agen Kolar"), and [Saesee Tiin](/wiki/Saesee_Tiin "Saesee Tiin") to [arrest the Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office"). The mission ended in failure, with Sidious cutting down all but Windu, and Skywalker himself arriving just as Windu gained the upper hand on Sidious. Believing that the Sith possessed the power to save Amidala, Skywalker betrayed Windu by helping Sidious take him out, before betraying the Jedi as a whole and kneeling before the Sith Master. Thus, Sidious had used Skywalker's anger with the Council and fear of losing Amidala to turn him to the dark side of the Force, making the Jedi's own Chosen One into his new Sith apprentice, Darth Vader.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9)

 [![Through Order 66, the Sith initiated a galaxy-wide purge that rendered the Jedi virtually extinct.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bd/Grogus_Flashback.png/revision/latest?cb=20220203030132) [![Through Order 66, the Sith initiated a galaxy-wide purge that rendered the Jedi virtually extinct.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bd/Grogus_Flashback.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220203030132)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bd/Grogus_Flashback.png/revision/latest?cb=20220203030132) 

Through Order 66, the Sith initiated a galaxy-wide purge that rendered the Jedi virtually extinct.

 

To launch the [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge"), Sidious ordered the clone troopers across the galaxy to execute [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"),[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) which branded the Jedi and any clone who tried to help them as traitors who needed to be executed. Many of the clone troopers had befriended their Jedi leadership, but their loyalty was forcibly erased due to their biochips, which Sidious and Dooku had implanted in the clones during their youth. With Sidious issuing the order, this activated the clones' biochips, which brainwashed them into believing that the Jedi were traitors to the Republic, leading to them turning on their Jedi commanders.[[117]](#cite_note-Shattered-117) Jedi across the galaxy were therefore betrayed and gunned down by their own soldiers. Additionally, Vader [led](/wiki/Operation:_Knightfall "Operation: Knightfall")[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) his elite[[118]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-118) [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion") into the Jedi Temple itself, murdering everyone, even the younglings, they found inside.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) Though Order 66 only explicitly targeted the Jedi, other Force-sensitives would find themselves in its crosshairs; Maul and Tano were both targeted aboard the [*Venator*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer") *[Tribunal](/wiki/Tribunal "Tribunal")* by the [332nd Division](/wiki/332nd_Division "332nd Division"), though Maul escaped aboard a [*Nu*-class transport](/wiki/Nu-class_attack/transport_shuttle "Nu-class attack/transport shuttle"), while Tano and [Clone Captain](/wiki/Clone_Captain "Clone Captain") [CT-7567](/wiki/Rex "Rex") "Rex," whose control chip had been removed by the former Padawan, fled aboard a [BTL-B Y-wing starfighter/bomber](/wiki/BTL-B_Y-wing_starfighter/bomber "BTL-B Y-wing starfighter/bomber") as the *Tribunal* crashed.[[119]](#cite_note-Victory_and_Death-119)

As Vader cut down the [Separatist Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council") on the volcanic world of [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar"), as per the command of Sidious, who betrayed and orchestrated the Council's death, Sidious used Windu's strike against him as an excuse to brand the Jedi as traitors before vowing to hunt down the surviving members of the Order and [transforming the Republic](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") into his [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"). Yoda tried to rescue the galaxy from the new Sith Emperor, but he was not able to kill Sidious, and went into exile. When Amidala confronted her husband on Mustafar, he was enraged to see Kenobi, who had secretly stowed away aboard her [J-type Naboo star skiff](/wiki/J-type_Naboo_star_skiff "J-type Naboo star skiff"). After encasing Amidala in a [Force choke](/wiki/Force_choke "Force choke"), Kenobi and Vader engaged in a [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Duel_on_Mustafar "Duel on Mustafar"), which ended when Kenobi left Vader to die near a lava river. A short time later, Amidala died in childbirth, with her two children, [Luke](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker") and [Leia](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"), separated to keep them safe. Leia was taken to live with the [House of Organa](/wiki/House_of_Organa "House of Organa") on [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan"), while Luke was taken to Tatooine to live with his aunt and uncle, [Beru](/wiki/Beru_Whitesun_Lars "Beru Whitesun Lars") and [Owen Lars](/wiki/Owen_Lars "Owen Lars"), while being watched over by Kenobi. Meanwhile, Vader had survived as well and was given a [suit of life support armor](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_armor "Darth Vader's armor") to survive.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) Immediately after his reconstruction, Sidious tasked Vader with taking a [kyber crystal](/wiki/Kyber_crystal "Kyber crystal") from a Jedi to [bleed](/wiki/Bleeding "Bleeding") it to be his own.[[120]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_1-120)

 [![The remaining Jedi were hunted by the Sith Lord Darth Vader, who was once the Jedi Knight Anakin Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Darth_Vader_Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_3_Textless.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170420140400) [![The remaining Jedi were hunted by the Sith Lord Darth Vader, who was once the Jedi Knight Anakin Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Darth_Vader_Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_3_Textless.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20170420140400)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Darth_Vader_Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_3_Textless.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170420140400) 

The remaining Jedi were hunted by the Sith Lord Darth Vader, who was once the Jedi Knight Anakin Skywalker.

 

Needing to find a Jedi who had survived the purge, Vader used the database on the Jedi [space station](/wiki/Space_station "Space station") *[Brighthome](/wiki/Brighthome "Brighthome")* to locate a Jedi who had taken the [Barash Vow](/wiki/Barash_Vow "Barash Vow"), pointing him to Jedi Master [Kirak Infil'a](/wiki/Kirak_Infil%27a "Kirak Infil'a")[[121]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_2-121) on the [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories") river [moon](/wiki/Moon "Moon") of [Al'doleem](/wiki/Al%27doleem "Al'doleem"). After arriving,[[122]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_3-122) Vader and Infil'a [began a duel](/wiki/Mission_to_Al%27doleem "Mission to Al'doleem") that ended with the Sith Lord killing the Jedi Master and flooding the [city](/wiki/Am%27balaar_City "Am'balaar City") below. Vader also successfully stole [his lightsaber](/wiki/Kirak_Infil%27a%27s_lightsaber "Kirak Infil'a's lightsaber") for its kyber crystal.[[123]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_4-123) Thus, as Sidious ordered, Vader went to Mustafar to bleed the crystal to his will.
