Though it presented the Sith Lord with a vision where he returned to the light side of the Force, Vader rejected this and twisted the crystal to the dark side.[[124]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_5-124) Meanwhile, word spread throughout the galaxy's population that the Jedi had apparently betrayed the Republic and that their Order had been destroyed for it.[[125]](#cite_note-K2-125) Organa launched an [investigation into the framing of the Jedi](/wiki/Investigation_into_the_framing_of_the_Jedi "Investigation into the framing of the Jedi") on the belief that, if he could prove Palpatine's evidence against the Jedi was fabricated, the Imperial project would collapse and justice would be served to the Jedi. However, his designs fell apart with the death of the Separatist [cyborg](/wiki/Cyborg "Cyborg") [assassin](/wiki/Assassin "Assassin") [Soujen Vak-Nhalis](/wiki/Soujen_Vak-Nhalis "Soujen Vak-Nhalis"), whose [databanks](/wiki/Databank "Databank") had contained the evidence Organa hoped to use.[[116]](#cite_note-MoF-116)

### The Jedi Purge

:   "*We seek a dangerous fugitive. This is no common anarchist but a devotee of the treasonous Jedi Order. Failure to turn over this traitor will result in a charge of sedition. Turn yourself in or everyone present shall face summary execution.*"
:   ―[Second Sister](/wiki/Second_Sister "Second Sister")[[13]](#cite_note-JFO-13)

The Empire's official explanation for the end of the Clone Wars[[105]](#cite_note-Catalyst-105) correctly stated that[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) the Jedi had been killed in massive numbers, with the Empire stating it was by the thousands, that the Jedi Temple had been the site of a battle, and that the few survivors had fled throughout space. However, they also claimed the Force had dispersed. Though this explanation was not universally accepted, most people in the galaxy accepted the destruction of the Jedi, just as they had accepted the sacrifices of the clones, if it meant the war was over. To [Lyra Erso](/wiki/Lyra_Erso "Lyra Erso"), it seemed as though mere [weeks](/wiki/Standard_week "Standard week") passed before, without much grief or mourning, the Jedi Order had almost entirely been reduced to a myth.[[105]](#cite_note-Catalyst-105) In fact, many celebrated the destruction of the Jedi,[[120]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_1-120) having believed Sidious's claims of a Jedi rebellion[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) and other Imperial propaganda[[120]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_1-120) that firmly squared the galaxy's recent troubles on the Order.[[126]](#cite_note-Launchpad229-126) Other citizens, meanwhile, simply blamed the Jedi for failing to prevent the Clone Wars or to more quickly end it.[[127]](#cite_note-MaskFear-127)

Using fear, new laws, and its vast military, the Empire worked to crush surviving Jedi and their remaining supporters, creating such a fear about even discussing the Jedi that knowledge of them died off, as it was not passed down.[[36]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_3-36) It was illegal to help Jedi during the Imperial Era; the [parents](/wiki/Parent "Parent") of [Dak Ralter](/wiki/Dak_Ralter "Dak Ralter") were given lifelong sentences for smuggling surviving Jedi Knights to safety.[[128]](#cite_note-Against_All_Odds-128) Due to the Empire's interest in eliminating the Jedi, rewards were offered to those who surrendered them.[[13]](#cite_note-JFO-13) Regardless of whether he was alive or dead, a Jedi could yield a high reward to a [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter").[[129]](#cite_note-129) Surviving Jedi who tried to uphold the Order's ways became known as [Jedi Arbiters](/wiki/Jedi_Arbiter "Jedi Arbiter"),[[130]](#cite_note-Disciples-130) with those they trained out in the galaxy described as [Bokken Jedi](/wiki/Bokken_Jedi "Bokken Jedi") by the fallen Jedi [Baylan Skoll](/wiki/Baylan_Skoll "Baylan Skoll").[[131]](#cite_note-Part_Six-131) [Vanzell Mar-Klar](/wiki/Vanzell_Mar-Klar "Vanzell Mar-Klar") and their Padawan, [Nedriss Narr](/wiki/Nedriss_Narr "Nedriss Narr"), tried to train a new generation of Knights in a hidden temple.[[132]](#cite_note-Trials-132) However, other survivors were mentally beaten and decided to simply survive in the new era, rather than use their abilities for the common good.[[13]](#cite_note-JFO-13)

 [![Inquisitors were fallen Jedi who hunted their former brethren as agents of the Sith and the Galactic Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/OrderOfInquisitors-PromiseOfPower.png/revision/latest?cb=20251112154624) [![Inquisitors were fallen Jedi who hunted their former brethren as agents of the Sith and the Galactic Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/OrderOfInquisitors-PromiseOfPower.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20251112154624)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/OrderOfInquisitors-PromiseOfPower.png/revision/latest?cb=20251112154624) 

Inquisitors were fallen Jedi who hunted their former brethren as agents of the Sith and the Galactic Empire.

 

With Order 66 still in effect,[[133]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_5-133) the Empire continued to hunt Jedi who had survived the protocol, with Sidious establishing the [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius") to seek out and kill the survivors.[[134]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_6-134) The next survivor Vader [encountered](/wiki/Hunt_for_Jocasta_Nu "Hunt for Jocasta Nu") was former [Chief Librarian](/wiki/Chief_Librarian "Chief Librarian") [Jocasta Nu](/wiki/Jocasta_Nu "Jocasta Nu"),[[135]](#cite_note-Dying_Light_II-135) who had recorded her knowledge in [holocrons](/wiki/Holocron "Holocron") in a [secret collection](/wiki/Jocasta_Nu%27s_cache "Jocasta Nu's cache") away from Imperial eyes. She returned to Coruscant to prevent the Empire from discovering a [Kyber memory crystal](/wiki/Kyber_memory_crystal "Kyber memory crystal") list of Force-sensitive children,[[136]](#cite_note-Dying_Light_I-136) leading to her conflict with Vader and the Inquisitors. After her capture, she revealed the Emperor wanted her alive to access the list of children, whom he would turn into more dark side servants. Vader arranged for her death and destroyed the crystal, preventing such a future.[[137]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_10-137) Over the years, Vader and the Inquisitorius hunted down what remained of the Jedi Order.[[58]](#cite_note-Twilight_of_the_Apprentice-58) Additionally, a Force-sensitive criminal named [Kilmera Skale](/wiki/Kilmera_Skale "Kilmera Skale"), who allied with [ISB](/wiki/Imperial_Security_Bureau "Imperial Security Bureau") [Special Agent](/wiki/Special_Agent "Special Agent") [Malor Phiatt](/wiki/Malor_Phiatt "Malor Phiatt"), pretended to be a Jedi to entrap those who survived the execution of Order 66.[[138]](#cite_note-EV-138)

A year into the Empire's reign in [18 BBY](/wiki/18_BBY "18 BBY"),[[139]](#cite_note-18_BBY_date-139) the eighty-third [King of Mon Cala](/wiki/King_of_Mon_Cala "King of Mon Cala"), [Lee-Char](/wiki/Lee-Char "Lee-Char"),[[140]](#cite_note-Prisoners-140) was manipulated by [Ferren Barr](/wiki/Ferren_Barr "Ferren Barr"),[[141]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_17-141) a surviving Padawan who had turned away from the path of the Jedi in order to destroy the Sith.[[142]](#cite_note-TSWB-142) Although he and the majority of his [disciples](/wiki/Ferren_Barr%27s_disciples "Ferren Barr's disciples") were killed by Vader and his forces during the [Imperial invasion of Mon Cala](/wiki/Invasion_of_Mon_Cala "Invasion of Mon Cala"), Barr [died](/wiki/Duel_in_the_Royal_Command_Bunker "Duel in the Royal Command Bunker") having ensured [Mon Calamari](/wiki/Mon_Calamari "Mon Calamari") starships would [rebel against the Empire](/wiki/Defense_of_the_southern_polar_regions "Defense of the southern polar regions"). Barr had also recruited the Force-sensitive [Verla](/wiki/Verla "Verla") as his apprentice,[[141]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_17-141) but, even though she survived the invasion, she would eventually give up on the Jedi path, choosing to go into hiding instead.[[143]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2020_6-143)

 [![Though hunted by Inquisitors, Cal Kestis sought to restore the fallen order by training a new generation of Jedi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/CalVsTrilla.png/revision/latest?cb=20210519104858) [![Though hunted by Inquisitors, Cal Kestis sought to restore the fallen order by training a new generation of Jedi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/CalVsTrilla.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210519104858)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/CalVsTrilla.png/revision/latest?cb=20210519104858) 

Though hunted by Inquisitors, Cal Kestis sought to restore the fallen order by training a new generation of Jedi.

 

In [14 BBY](/wiki/14_BBY "14 BBY"),[[144]](#cite_note-14_BBY_Note-144) the Padawan [Cal Kestis](/wiki/Cal_Kestis "Cal Kestis"), after being discovered by the Empire and escaping the Inquisitors at [Bracca](/wiki/Bracca "Bracca"), joined former Jedi Knight [Cere Junda](/wiki/Cere_Junda "Cere Junda") on a quest to restore the Jedi Order. Both searched for a [holocron](/wiki/Eno_Cordova%27s_holocron "Eno Cordova's holocron") containing a list of Force-sensitive youth across the galaxy, which was hidden by Jedi Master [Eno Cordova](/wiki/Eno_Cordova "Eno Cordova"). Although they both obtained the holocron after a few clashes with the Inquisitors and one with Darth Vader, Kestis decided to destroy it to keep the young men on the list safe from the Empire.[[13]](#cite_note-JFO-13)

 [![Jedi Knight Tensu Run became a symbol of something the Empire could not tolerate: hope.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/TensuRunRegisKor-Inquisitors1.png/revision/latest?cb=20241217000142) [![Jedi Knight Tensu Run became a symbol of something the Empire could not tolerate: hope.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/TensuRunRegisKor-Inquisitors1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20241217000142)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/TensuRunRegisKor-Inquisitors1.png/revision/latest?cb=20241217000142) 

Jedi Knight Tensu Run became a symbol of something the Empire could not tolerate: hope.

 

Jedi Knight [Tensu Run](/wiki/Tensu_Run "Tensu Run") became a threat to the Empire, as after freeing prisoners from an [Imperial outpost](/wiki/Imperial_outpost_(Regis_Kor) "Imperial outpost (Regis Kor)") during the [Conquest of Regis Kor](/wiki/Conquest_of_Regis_Kor "Conquest of Regis Kor"), he became a symbol of hope. Tensu Run's [death](/wiki/Death "Death") became one of the Inquisitorius' highest priorities, with [the Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor"),[[145]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_1-145) the [Fifth Brother](/wiki/Fifth_Brother "Fifth Brother"),[[146]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_2-146) the [Seventh Sister](/wiki/Seventh_Sister "Seventh Sister") and the [Ninth Sister](/wiki/Ninth_Sister "Ninth Sister"),[[147]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_3-147) all participating in the [hunt](/wiki/Hunt_for_Tensu_Run "Hunt for Tensu Run"). The Inquisitors were defeated more than once by the Jedi Knight, who, along with other survivors of Order 66, sought to restore the Jedi Order. Due to the Inquisitors' failures, Darth Vader led the four Inquisitors in a final confrontation with the Jedi, which resulted in Run's death by the hands of the Sith Lord, as well as the other Jedi, who were killed by the Inquisitors.[[148]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_4-148)

 [![Cal Kestis became one of the most wanted Jedi by the Galactic Empire in 9 BBY.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/CalKestisSecondLightsaberCrossguard-Survivor.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20221210154909) [![Cal Kestis became one of the most wanted Jedi by the Galactic Empire in 9 BBY.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/CalKestisSecondLightsaberCrossguard-Survivor.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20221210154909)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/CalKestisSecondLightsaberCrossguard-Survivor.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20221210154909) 

Cal Kestis became one of the most wanted Jedi by the Galactic Empire in 9 BBY.

 

Over the five years following the holocron's destruction, Kestis has become an extremely important target for the Empire, having attracted the attention of not only the Inquisitorius, but the [ISB](/wiki/Imperial_Security_Bureau "Imperial Security Bureau") as well.[[149]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Jedi:_Survivor-149) In [9 BBY](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY"),[[150]](#cite_note-Survivor_Date-150) on the planet [Koboh](/wiki/Koboh "Koboh"), Kestis encountered something from the Jedi's golden age. Kestis encountered the Jedi [Dagan Gera](/wiki/Dagan_Gera "Dagan Gera"), who has been preserved in bacta since the days of the High Republic. Kestis freed the old Jedi and asked for his help in his fight against the Empire. However, Gera fell out with the Jedi Order, who he believed had betrayed him because the Jedi had given up on [Tanalorr](/wiki/Tanalorr "Tanalorr"), a hard-to-reach world Dagan had become obsessed with, after an [attack](/wiki/Attack_on_Tanalorr "Attack on Tanalorr") by the [Nihil](/wiki/Nihil "Nihil"). Gera fell to the dark side and bled the kyber crystal from his lightsaber, starting a duel with Kestis afterwards. Dagan escaped with the help of his old ally, the [Gen'Dai](/wiki/Gen%27Dai "Gen'Dai") [Rayvis](/wiki/Rayvis "Rayvis"), and intended to return to Tanalorr and create an army led by Force users trained by himself to fight the Empire. However, due to the clouded view of Gera by the dark side, Kestis opposed his plan. Along with [Bode Akuna](/wiki/Bode_Akuna "Bode Akuna"), Kestis killed Dagan and obtained the compass that would guide them to Tanalorr, a place that Kestis intended to transform into a refuge for those persecuted by the Empire.[[149]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Jedi:_Survivor-149)

 [![Dagan Gera, a High Republic-era Jedi who had been in suspended animation for centuries, was found and freed by Jedi Knight Cal Kestis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/Dagan_Gera.png/revision/latest?cb=20230616190645) [![Dagan Gera, a High Republic-era Jedi who had been in suspended animation for centuries, was found and freed by Jedi Knight Cal Kestis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/Dagan_Gera.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20230616190645)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/62/Dagan_Gera.png/revision/latest?cb=20230616190645) 

Dagan Gera, a High Republic-era Jedi who had been in suspended animation for centuries, was found and freed by Jedi Knight Cal Kestis.

 

However, the compass was stolen by Akuna, who was an ISB's spy and a survivor of the Jedi Purge. Akuna intended to flee to Tanalorr with his daughter so that they could live free from the Empire forever, which, in his opinion, Kestis' intentions for Tanalorr jeopardized. Kestis followed Akuna to Tanalorr, and along with his ally, the [Nightsister](/wiki/Nightsisters "Nightsisters") [Merrin](/wiki/Merrin "Merrin"), slew him. Kestis and his friends took in Bode's daughter and held a Jedi funeral for Akuna, Cere Junda, and Eno Cordova, who were trying to restore knowledge from the Jedi archives and were killed due to Akuna stealing the compass. Having the compass, Kestis and his allies began to prepare Tanalorr for use by [Hidden Path](/wiki/Hidden_Path "Hidden Path").[[149]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Jedi:_Survivor-149)

In [5 BBY](/wiki/5_BBY "5 BBY"),[[151]](#cite_note-Spark_Date-151) one survivor, [Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus"), formerly known as the Padawan Caleb Dume,[[152]](#cite_note-Kanan_1-152) took on a Padawan of his own, [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger"). Both of them worked as part of the [Spectres](/wiki/Spectres "Spectres"), a rebel crew based out of the [VCX-100 light freighter](/wiki/VCX-100_light_freighter "VCX-100 light freighter") *[Ghost](/wiki/Ghost "Ghost")* that often struck at the Empire on [Lothal](/wiki/Lothal "Lothal").[[153]](#cite_note-Spark-153) During the [action at Mustafar](/wiki/Action_at_Mustafar "Action at Mustafar"), Jarrus and Bridger confronted [the Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor"), who chose to take his own life instead of facing the wrath of his masters for failing to defeat them. The Spectres then joined up with the larger [Phoenix Cell](/wiki/Phoenix_Cell "Phoenix Cell"), which let Jarrus and Bridger work with Ahsoka Tano, who had become a [Fulcrum](/wiki/Fulcrum "Fulcrum") agent for [Bail Organa's resistance movement](/wiki/Bail_Organa%27s_resistance_movement "Bail Organa's resistance movement") and the overall growing rebellion. These rebel cells entered into a [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War") against the Empire.[[15]](#cite_note-Fire_Across_the_Galaxy-15)

 [![Vader confronted his former apprentice, the former Jedi Ahsoka Tano, in a Sith temple on Malachor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d4/218-AhsokavVader.png/revision/latest?cb=20240402200301) [![Vader confronted his former apprentice, the former Jedi Ahsoka Tano, in a Sith temple on Malachor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d4/218-AhsokavVader.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20240402200301)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d4/218-AhsokavVader.png/revision/latest?cb=20240402200301) 

Vader confronted his former apprentice, the former Jedi Ahsoka Tano, in a Sith temple on Malachor.

 

Master [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") had also survived the purge, having survived both Order 66 and a [duel in the Galactic Senate](/wiki/Duel_in_the_Galactic_Senate "Duel in the Galactic Senate") against Sidious.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) He based himself on the remote planet of [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah "Dagobah") to avoid Imperial hunters,[[89]](#cite_note-USW-89) though he was able to connect with the Lothal Jedi on two occasions through the [World Between Worlds](/wiki/World_Between_Worlds "World Between Worlds").[[154]](#cite_note-POTJ-154)[[115]](#cite_note-Shroud_of_Darkness-115) On the second occasion, Tano learned Vader was in fact her former mentor Skywalker, Yoda told Bridger to go to Malachor when he asked for advice on fighting the Sith, and Jarrus was knighted by a vision of the Grand Inquisitor.[[115]](#cite_note-Shroud_of_Darkness-115) During the [Mission to Malachor](/wiki/Mission_to_Malachor "Mission to Malachor"), Tano finally encountered Vader. She again affirmed she was not a Jedi in order to seek revenge for her mentor's demise, as Skywalker had effectively died when he became Vader. At the end of their duel, Tano was presumed dead at Vader's hands,[[58]](#cite_note-Twilight_of_the_Apprentice-58) but she had actually been saved by Bridger sometime later using the World Between Worlds.[[155]](#cite_note-AWBW-155)

Before he reached the point in his life where he rescued Tano, Bridger and the other rebels lived through much.[[155]](#cite_note-AWBW-155) In [2 BBY](/wiki/2_BBY "2 BBY"),[[10]](#cite_note-Timelines-10)[[156]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns_date-156) the Spectres and other rebel cells officially formed into the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic"),[[157]](#cite_note-Secret_Cargo-157) and the former Sith Lord Maul was [struck down](/wiki/Mission_to_Tatooine_(Imperial_Era) "Mission to Tatooine (Imperial Era)") on Tatooine by his old nemesis, Obi-Wan Kenobi. Before dying in his enemy's arms, Maul asked if the individual Kenobi was guarding on the desert world was the Chosen One. Believing Luke Skywalker was, Kenobi said as such, giving Maul hope that they would be avenged.[[158]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-158)

 [![The Jedi Ezra Bridger went missing after the liberation of his home planet of Lothal.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Ezra_before_being_sent_into_hyperspace.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220513143208) [![The Jedi Ezra Bridger went missing after the liberation of his home planet of Lothal.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Ezra_before_being_sent_into_hyperspace.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220513143208)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Ezra_before_being_sent_into_hyperspace.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220513143208) 

The Jedi Ezra Bridger went missing after the liberation of his home planet of Lothal.

 

In [1 BBY](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY"),[[10]](#cite_note-Timelines-10) Jarrus's lover,[[159]](#cite_note-Jedi_Night-159) General [Hera Syndulla](/wiki/Hera_Syndulla "Hera Syndulla"), was captured after a failed Rebel Alliance [assault](/wiki/Attack_on_Lothal "Attack on Lothal") on the heavily-occupied Lothal.[[160]](#cite_note-Rebel_Assault-160) Jarrus was able to [rescue](/wiki/Rescue_of_Hera_Syndulla_(Lothal) "Rescue of Hera Syndulla (Lothal)") her, but he soon had to give his life to protect Bridger, Syndulla, and the Mandalorian [Sabine Wren](/wiki/Sabine_Wren "Sabine Wren").[[159]](#cite_note-Jedi_Night-159) A short time later, Bridger entered the World Between Worlds and rescued Tano. While making sure Sidious would be unable to secure the power of the World Between Worlds, Tano and Bridger again parted ways, with Tano promising to find him when the time came.[[155]](#cite_note-AWBW-155) Bridger then led the [effort to liberate](/wiki/Liberation_of_Lothal "Liberation of Lothal") his homeworld of Lothal. During the battle, Bridger spoke with [Grand Admiral](/wiki/Grand_Admiral "Grand Admiral") [Thrawn](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo"), who stated the Jedi had been reduced to those who were beaten, hidden away, or inexpertly trained Padawans. After again denying Sidious entrance into the World Between Worlds and having had a pod of [purrgil](/wiki/Purrgil "Purrgil") summoned to Lothal, Bridger used [beast control](/wiki/Taming_beasts "Taming beasts") to have the creatures take him, Thrawn, and the Star Destroyer *[Chimaera](/wiki/Chimaera "Chimaera")* away[[161]](#cite_note-Family&Farewell-161) to deep space.[[162]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars_NE-162) Though Bridger's disappearance took another Jedi out of galactic affairs, the purrgil had taken out the [7th Fleet](/wiki/Seventh_Fleet_(Galactic_Empire) "Seventh Fleet (Galactic Empire)"), and the Padawan's effort against Thrawn had successfully liberated Lothal.[[161]](#cite_note-Family&Farewell-161)

### Rebirth of the Jedi

#### Luke Skywalker joins the Rebellion

:   "*The Jedi are extinct. Their fire has gone out of the universe. You, my friend, are all that's left of their religion.*"
:   ―Wilhuff Tarkin, to Darth Vader[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4)

When it seemed as though the Jedi had been destroyed, the Imperial [Inquisitors](/wiki/Inquisitor "Inquisitor") vanished as well.[[51]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-51) [Grand Moff](/wiki/Grand_Moff "Grand Moff") [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin"), a member of the Empire's leading triumvirate along with Darth Vader and Emperor Palpatine,[[163]](#cite_note-Tarkin-163) considered Vader the last remnant of the Jedi faith,[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4) although four of the Rebellion's [guiding principles](/wiki/Alliance_guiding_principles "Alliance guiding principles") were near-quotations of Jedi texts.[[164]](#cite_note-EA1-164) Additionally, [Imperial officer](/wiki/Imperial_officer "Imperial officer") [Arvira](/wiki/Arvira "Arvira") of the [logistics corps](/wiki/Logistics_corps "Logistics corps") believed even saying the word "Jedi" in Imperial territory was unadvisable.[[165]](#cite_note-The_Sith_of_Datawork-165)

In 1 BBY,[[166]](#cite_note-IV_Date-166) in the midst of the Galactic Civil War and after the [Battle of Scarif](/wiki/Battle_of_Scarif "Battle of Scarif"), Luke Skywalker finally became a part of the wider galaxy when [protocol droid](/wiki/Protocol_droid "Protocol droid") [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO "C-3PO") and [astromech droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid") [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2") arrived on Tatooine.[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4) Both droids had known his father, Anakin Skywalker, before his fall, but C-3PO's memory of such events had been wiped.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) R2-D2 was in possession of the [plans](/wiki/Death_Star_plans "Death Star plans") to the [DS-1 Death Star Mobile Battle Station](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station"), an Imperial [superweapon](/wiki/Superweapon "Superweapon") powerful enough to destroy an entire planet. The plans had been entrusted to him by[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4) Skywalker's sister, [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") Leia Organa. Both siblings remained unaware of each other thanks to their separate upbringings,[[34]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-34) and Skywalker first saw her when R2 projected a hologram of her.[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4)

 [![Luke Skywalker began his Jedi training under Obi-Wan Kenobi, the Jedi Master who trained his father, Anakin Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/Darth_Maul_2_Star_Wars_40th.png/revision/latest?cb=20190119011903) [![Luke Skywalker began his Jedi training under Obi-Wan Kenobi, the Jedi Master who trained his father, Anakin Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/Darth_Maul_2_Star_Wars_40th.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190119011903)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/Darth_Maul_2_Star_Wars_40th.png/revision/latest?cb=20190119011903) 

Luke Skywalker began his Jedi training under Obi-Wan Kenobi, the Jedi Master who trained his father, Anakin Skywalker.

 

Organa also gave the droid orders to find Obi-Wan Kenobi on Tatooine, whom Skywalker had met over his years on the desert world. Meeting with him, Kenobi presented Skywalker with [Anakin's lightsaber](/wiki/Skywalker_lightsaber "Skywalker lightsaber") and[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4) avoided telling the complete truth[[167]](#cite_note-Master_and_Apprentice-167) about Anakin by claiming Vader had killed him. After[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4) a stormtrooper execution [squad](/wiki/Squad "Squad")[[89]](#cite_note-USW-89) killed Owen and Beru Lars, Skywalker joined Kenobi on his journey to return R2-D2 and C-3PO to Alderaan, hiring [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo") and his [First Mate](/wiki/First_Mate "First Mate"), the [Wookiee](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") [Chewbacca](/wiki/Chewbacca "Chewbacca"), to transport them aboard their [YT-1300 light freighter](/wiki/YT-1300_light_freighter "YT-1300 light freighter"), the *[Millennium Falcon](/wiki/Millennium_Falcon "Millennium Falcon")*.[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4)

Skywalker began his Jedi training during their journey, though Solo was outspoken in his belief that the Force did not exist. However, before they reached the planet, Tarkin ordered the Death Star [to destroy](/wiki/Destruction_of_Alderaan "Destruction of Alderaan") Alderaan, sending out a [disturbance in the Force](/wiki/Disturbance_in_the_Force "Disturbance in the Force") made up of the millions of screaming [Alderaanians](/wiki/Alderaanian "Alderaanian") killed in the explosion. Upon arriving at the planet's remains, the crew of the *Millennium Falcon* were taken aboard the Death Star by a [tractor beam](/wiki/Tractor_beam "Tractor beam"). Onboard, Skywalker convinced Solo to help him [rescue Organa](/wiki/Rescue_of_Princess_Leia "Rescue of Princess Leia"), while Kenobi confronted Vader. To give Skywalker and the others a chance to escape, Kenobi sacrificed himself, dying at the hands of his former apprentice but becoming one with the Force. When the Empire tracked the *Millennium Falcon* to the [Rebel Alliance's base](/wiki/Great_Temple "Great Temple") on the moon of [Yavin 4](/wiki/Yavin_4 "Yavin 4"), Skywalker joined [the battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin") to destroy the Death Star, flying in [Red Five](/wiki/Red_Five_(T-65B_X-wing_starfighter) "Red Five (T-65B X-wing starfighter)") with R2-D2[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4) and leading [fourth flight](/wiki/Fourth_flight "Fourth flight").[[168]](#cite_note-Duty_Roster-168) After Solo knocked Vader away, Skywalker listened to the voice of Kenobi, using the Force to help fire two [proton torpedoes](/wiki/Proton_torpedo "Proton torpedo") into a [thermal exhaust port](/wiki/Thermal_exhaust_port "Thermal exhaust port").[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4)

With the Death Star destroyed,[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4) Skywalker and his friends became known as the "[Heroes of Yavin](/wiki/Heroes_of_Yavin "Heroes of Yavin")."[[169]](#cite_note-HC_12-169) A short time after the Battle of Yavin, they fought in the [attack on Cymoon 1](/wiki/Assault_on_Cymoon "Assault on Cymoon"), during which he confronted Vader for the death of Kenobi and alleged death of his father. During their brief encounter, Vader realized Skywalker wielded his old lightsaber.[[170]](#cite_note-Skywalker_Strikes_Part_II-170) Intending to learn the identity of his new enemy, whom he realized was the same pilot[[171]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_1-171) who had destroyed the Death Star,[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4) Vader hired [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Boba Fett](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett") to learn his identity and capture him.[[171]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_1-171) When Skywalker [returned to Tatooine](/wiki/Duel_in_Ben_Kenobi%27s_home "Duel in Ben Kenobi's home") to recover [Kenobi's journals](/wiki/The_Journals_of_Ben_Kenobi "The Journals of Ben Kenobi"), he escaped Fett,[[172]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_6-172) but the bounty hunter had still learned his name. That information taught Vader that he had a son, inspiring him[[173]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_6-173) to one day overthrow the Emperor with his son at his side.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_V-2)

#### Apprentice without a Jedi Master

:   "*Remember, the Force will be with you always.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi's spirit, to Luke Skywalker[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-4)

Seeking passage to the Jedi Temple on Coruscant, Skywalker and R2-D2 [arrived on the "Smuggler's Moon"](/wiki/Rescue_of_Luke_Skywalker "Rescue of Luke Skywalker") of [Nar Shaddaa](/wiki/Nar_Shaddaa "Nar Shaddaa").[[174]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_8-174) The young Jedi was captured by [Grakkus Jahibakti Tingi](/wiki/Grakkus_Jahibakti_Tingi "Grakkus Jahibakti Tingi"), a [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt") [crime lord](/wiki/Crime_lord "Crime lord") who collected Jedi artifacts that he claimed to be the last remnants of the Order. When Grakkus forced Skywalker to open a Jedi holocron, he accidentally opened the Hutt's entire holocron collection, convincing Grakkus that Skywalker was the last of the Jedi.[[18]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_9-18) Thus, the crime lord plotted for a colosseum match between the young Force-sensitive and a beast, eventually choosing[[175]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_10-175) a [Roggwart](/wiki/Roggwart "Roggwart")[[176]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-176) named [Kongo](/wiki/Kongo "Kongo"). After a training against with "[the Gamemaster](/wiki/Kreel "Kreel")," who taught Skywalker that the Coruscant Jedi Temple had been converted into Palpatine's palace, and [IG-100 MagnaGuards](/wiki/IG-100_MagnaGuard "IG-100 MagnaGuard"),[[175]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_10-175) Grakkus forced Skywalker, introduced to the crowd as "the last of the Jedi," into the colosseum,[[177]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_11-177) but the match was cut short when the Gamemaster activated Kongo's shock collar. In reality, he was an undercover stormtrooper [sergeant](/wiki/Sergeant "Sergeant") named Kreel, as the Empire had taken notice of Grakkus's stockpile of Jedi artifacts.[[178]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_12-178)

 [![Skywalker, bereft of a master after Kenobi's death, searched for knowledge in the ruins of other Jedi temples across the galaxy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/VrogasVasRuins-VaderDown1.png/revision/latest?cb=20180213012509) [![Skywalker, bereft of a master after Kenobi's death, searched for knowledge in the ruins of other Jedi temples across the galaxy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/VrogasVasRuins-VaderDown1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180213012509)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/VrogasVasRuins-VaderDown1.png/revision/latest?cb=20180213012509) 

Skywalker, bereft of a master after Kenobi's death, searched for knowledge in the ruins of other Jedi temples across the galaxy.

 

Kreel was reinforced by a group of [TIE fighter pilots](/wiki/Imperial_Starfighter_Pilot "Imperial Starfighter Pilot"), but Grakkus activated a [electromagnetic pulse](/wiki/Electromagnetic_pulse "Electromagnetic pulse"), knocking out their blasters and Kongo's collar. When two pilots tried to arrest Skywalker, R2-D2 threw him his lightsaber, doing the same for Solo, Organa, and Chewbacca when they arrived by launching out sabers from Grakkus's collection. When Kreel was distracted by Grakkus, the rebels were given a chance to escape, although the stormtrooper still reported everything he had learned about the young Jedi to Vader.[[178]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_12-178) Having learned about a [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_(Vrogas_Vas) "Jedi Temple (Vrogas Vas)")[[18]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_9-18) on the planet[[179]](#cite_note-Vader_Down_1-179) [Vrogas Vas](/wiki/Vrogas_Vas "Vrogas Vas") from one of Grakkus's holocrons[[18]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_9-18) and reading about it in Kenobi's journal,[[180]](#cite_note-Vader_Down_5-180) Skywalker traveled to the world, but Vader learned of his journey from his agent, [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") [Chelli Lona Aphra](/wiki/Chelli_Lona_Aphra "Chelli Lona Aphra").[[181]](#cite_note-Shadows_and_Secrets,_Part_VI-181) During the [Battle of Vrogas Vas](/wiki/Battle_of_Vrogas_Vas "Battle of Vrogas Vas"), Skywalker was unable to focus on learning from the Jedi Temple with Vader on the ground, and the Sith Lord killed many [Rebel pilots](/wiki/Rebel_pilot "Rebel pilot")[[179]](#cite_note-Vader_Down_1-179) and [troopers](/wiki/Rebel_trooper "Rebel trooper") in his pursuit of his son.[[182]](#cite_note-Vader_Down_2-182)

While in the temple, Skywalker felt the presences of Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker, but he was then engaged by Aphra and Vader's two [assassin droids](/wiki/Assassin_droid "Assassin droid"), [0-0-0](/wiki/0-0-0 "0-0-0") and [BT-1](/wiki/BT-1 "BT-1").[[182]](#cite_note-Vader_Down_2-182) With the help of his friends, Skywalker escaped these agents.[[183]](#cite_note-SW13-183) Later, as he again walked through the temple, he heard Kenobi's voice and was warned that he should not have come to Vrogas Vas. Meanwhile, Vader dueled his rival, Commander [Karbin](/wiki/Karbin "Karbin"), and heard voices from his Jedi past.[[180]](#cite_note-Vader_Down_5-180) Though the Sith Lord managed to kill Karbin, Skywalker and his friends escaped the Empire and Vader's personal agents. However, Skywalker was saddened that he would never have the chance to return to the temple, believing he had been close to a uncovering a secret.[[184]](#cite_note-Vader_Down_6-184)

At some point after [investigating](/wiki/Mission_to_Vagadarr_Prime_(Luke_Skywalker) "Mission to Vagadarr Prime (Luke Skywalker)") a [planet](/wiki/Vagadarr_Prime "Vagadarr Prime") to see if it could help in his training, as the world had been mentioned in Kenobi's journal,[[185]](#cite_note-SW_28-185) and [fighting](/wiki/Mission_to_Ktath%27atn "Mission to Ktath'atn") the Force-sensitive [Queen of Ktath'atn](/wiki/Unidentified_Queen_of_Ktath%27atn "Unidentified Queen of Ktath'atn"),[[186]](#cite_note-Doctor_Aphra_8-186) Skywalker and his allies undertook a [mission](/wiki/Battle_for_Jedha "Battle for Jedha") to the ruins of Jedha[[187]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_38-187) in [1 ABY](/wiki/1_ABY "1 ABY").[[188]](#cite_note-Helmet_Collection_77-188) While on Jedha, he and [Chulco Gi](/wiki/Chulco_Gi "Chulco Gi"), who had wanted to join the [Disciples of the Whills](/wiki/Disciples_of_the_Whills "Disciples of the Whills"), journeyed to the [Temple of Central Isopter](/wiki/Temple_of_Central_Isopter "Temple of Central Isopter"), where the [death cult](/wiki/Central_Isopter "Central Isopter") claimed to Skywalker that, with the Jedi destroyed, their shrine was his only hope at learning the Force. Although he gazed into the crater, Skywalker did not want to lose himself to darkness, but Gi was corrupted by the abyss's connection to the dark side, forcing Skywalker to kill his companion in self-defense. Skywalker left the temple after the Central Isopter informed him the dark side could lead to madness if he did not have a proper guide, warning him to not fall because of his importance. Although he came to the conclusion that he might not end up a Jedi, but that he needed to be content with that, the mission on Jedha[[189]](#cite_note-Ashes_of_Jedha_4-189) would not be the last time Skywalker grabbled with that question.[[190]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_1-190)

#### The Redemptoin of Anakin Skywalker

:   "*No matter how far my father had fallen, I sensed that his turn to the dark side was not absolute. I knew Anakin Skywalker had followed his heart to a fault during his days as a Jedi. Our ultimate victory would rely on my belief that the same heart was still beating somewhere inside Darth Vader's armor.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker[[51]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-51)

Over five Dagobah days after his death, Obi-Wan Kenobi had appeared to Yoda as a [Force spirit](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit"), asking the Jedi Master to take on Skywalker as an apprentice. While Yoda had wanted to train Organa, he accepted Kenobi's request to train him.[[191]](#cite_note-There_is_Another-191) In [3 ABY](/wiki/3_ABY "3 ABY"), three years after the destruction of the Death Star,[[10]](#cite_note-Timelines-10) Skywalker journeyed to Dagobah with R2-D2 in the aftermath of the [Battle of Hoth](/wiki/Battle_of_Hoth "Battle of Hoth"), having been told by Kenobi's ghost to go here to train under the Jedi Master.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_V-2) Upon seeing the young man, Yoda felt the hope that he would be the next Jedi,[[192]](#cite_note-Age_of_Rebellion-192) although Skywalker's initial lack of patience nearly convinced the Jedi Master to reject him as an apprentice. Convinced to continue by Kenobi and Skywalker's protests, Yoda trained the young human[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_V-2) for several [weeks](/wiki/Standard_week "Standard week")[[193]](#cite_note-There_is_Always_Another-193) until the prodigy felt his friends being [tortured](/wiki/Torture "Torture") through the Force.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_V-2)

 [![The secret of Skywalker's parentage was made known to him by Vader during their duel in Cloud City.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/LukeVSVaderB.png/revision/latest?cb=20130324214148) [![The secret of Skywalker's parentage was made known to him by Vader during their duel in Cloud City.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/LukeVSVaderB.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130324214148)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/LukeVSVaderB.png/revision/latest?cb=20130324214148) 

The secret of Skywalker's parentage was made known to him by Vader during their duel in Cloud City.

 

Ignoring Kenobi and Yoda's protests but promising to one day return, Skywalker [traveled](/wiki/Escape_from_Cloud_City "Escape from Cloud City") to [Cloud City](/wiki/Cloud_City "Cloud City") on the world of [Bespin](/wiki/Bespin "Bespin"), where he [dueled and was bested](/wiki/Duel_on_Cloud_City "Duel on Cloud City") by Vader. After losing his hand and lightsaber during the duel, Skywalker was horrified when the Sith Lord revealed he was his father, choosing to fall down an air shaft rather than agree to Vader’s offer to rule the galaxy with him. After being rescued by his friends—who had lost Solo after the captain had been [frozen](/wiki/Carbon-freezing "Carbon-freezing") in [carbonite](/wiki/Carbonite "Carbonite") and taken away by Boba Fett—aboard the *Millennium Falcon*,[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_V-2) Skywalker was left in stunned silence over the truth of his heritage, not even noticing that Organa introduced his name to [Baron Administrator](/wiki/Baron_Administrator "Baron Administrator") [Landonis Balthazar Calrissian](/wiki/Landonis_Balthazar_Calrissian "Landonis Balthazar Calrissian").[[190]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_1-190)

After she informed him about recent events, while he only told her Kenobi had not answered his call for help in the Force, the *Millennium Falcon* traveled to Rebel [Rendezvous Point Delta-Three](/wiki/Rendezvous_Point_Delta-Three "Rendezvous Point Delta-Three"), forcing Skywalker and the others into an [Imperial ambush](/wiki/Battle_at_Rendezvous_Point_Delta-Three "Battle at Rendezvous Point Delta-Three") masterminded Commander [Ellian Zahra](/wiki/Ellian_Zahra "Ellian Zahra"). While manning one of the freighter's turrets, Skywalker, overwhelmed by the truth of his parentage, accidentally lashed out in the Force, helping take out[[190]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_1-190) a [squadron](/wiki/Squadron "Squadron")[[194]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2-194) of [TIE fighters](/wiki/TIE/ln_space_superiority_starfighter "TIE/ln space superiority starfighter"), which led to the [Fourth Division](/wiki/Fourth_Division "Fourth Division")'s successful escape to [Backup Rendezvous Point Gamma-Nine](/wiki/Backup_Rendezvous_Point_Gamma-Nine "Backup Rendezvous Point Gamma-Nine"). As the rebels discussed what to do aboard the [EF76 Nebulon-B escort frigate](/wiki/EF76_Nebulon-B_escort_frigate "EF76 Nebulon-B escort frigate") *[Redemption](/wiki/Redemption "Redemption")*, Skywalker stood alone with R2-D2, finding himself unable to connect with Yoda and questioning whether he should become a Jedi after all. Although scared as to what he could be if he was not to be a Jedi,[[190]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_1-190) he received a replacement hand aboard the *Redemption* and had a vision of a robed figure grabbing his fallen lightsaber on Cloud City.[[194]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2-194)

 [![Armed with a new lightsaber, Skywalker continued to train amid the Galactic Civil War.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/Star_Wars_2020_Vol_4_textless_cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211004203349) [![Armed with a new lightsaber, Skywalker continued to train amid the Galactic Civil War.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/Star_Wars_2020_Vol_4_textless_cover.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20211004203349)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/Star_Wars_2020_Vol_4_textless_cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211004203349) 

Armed with a new lightsaber, Skywalker continued to train amid the Galactic Civil War.

 

Unable to find his lightsaber after returning to Cloud City but deciding he would be a Jedi without it,[[195]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2020_4-195) Skywalker traveled to the planet [Serelia](/wiki/Serelia "Serelia") and located the woman he had seen in his visions, Verla;[[133]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_5-133) after spending years being hunted by the Empire, the former apprentice of Ferren Barr had abandoned the Jedi path to live in hiding. After learning Skywalker was not like his Sith father, Verla tried to dissuade him from following the Jedi path to avoid the pain it could cause, yet he remained steadfast in his desire to help the galaxy, promising to never visit her again if she gave the location of a [Jedi outpost](/wiki/Jedi_outpost_(Tempes) "Jedi outpost (Tempes)"). At the outpost on [Tempes](/wiki/Tempes "Tempes"), Skywalker located a [yellow lightsaber](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker%27s_yellow_lightsaber "Luke Skywalker's yellow lightsaber") but was confronted by the spirit of the [Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/Grand_Inquisitor "Grand Inquisitor"), who had been forced to remain in the mortal realm by Vader. Nevertheless, Skywalker defeated the specter, returning to the Fourth Division with R2-D2 and his new blade.[[143]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2020_6-143) Nevertheless, after using the blade against the Empire[[196]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2020_8-196) and in an effort to rescue Solo,[[197]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_13-197) Skywalker found himself in need of a [new lightsaber](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker%27s_green_lightsaber "Luke Skywalker's green lightsaber"), building a new weapon with a green blade.[[34]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-34)

Vader, meanwhile, had gone on a quest to find who exactly had hidden his son from him,[[198]](#cite_note-Vader_2020_1-198) yet his mission ultimately taught him what had happened to his wife, Padmé Amidala, and that, even in her final moments, she held faith that the light side still existed in him. Consumed with sadness instead of hatred, Vader returned to Coruscant,[[199]](#cite_note-Vader_2020_5-199) where he was tortured by Sidious for his lack of devotion to him. Leaving Vader on Mustafar as punishment,[[200]](#cite_note-Vader_2020_6-200) the Sith apprentice came to regain his strength, capturing Sidious's assassin, [Ochi of Bestoon](/wiki/Ochi "Ochi"), and traveling with him to the planet [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol"), where he had learned his master kept secrets.[[201]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_2020_10-201) Once on the Sith world, Vader proclaimed that he was no longer an apprentice, yet he was defeated by his master,[[202]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_2020_11-202) leaving him to feel that his son needed to die for the future of the Sith to unfold.[[203]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_2020_12-203)

 [![Amid the Battle of Endor, Skywalker and Vader dueled before the Emperor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/Conflict_and_Combat_FDCR.png/revision/latest?cb=20180630070544) [![Amid the Battle of Endor, Skywalker and Vader dueled before the Emperor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/Conflict_and_Combat_FDCR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180630070544)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/Conflict_and_Combat_FDCR.png/revision/latest?cb=20180630070544) 

Amid the Battle of Endor, Skywalker and Vader dueled before the Emperor.

 

After [freeing](/wiki/Rescue_of_Han_Solo "Rescue of Han Solo") Solo from carbonite and defeating crime lord [Jabba Desilijic Tiure](/wiki/Jabba_Desilijic_Tiure "Jabba Desilijic Tiure") on Tatooine, Skywalker returned to Dagobah, where Yoda became one with the Force, and the young Jedi learned Organa was his sister. Afterward, Skywalker promised to take part in the Rebel effort to destroy a [second Death Star](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station"), which was being constructed over the [forest](/wiki/Forest "Forest") moon of [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor"). Before the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor") could begin, however, he surrendered himself to Vader's custody, hoping he could turn his father back to the light side. Instead, the Sith Lord felt forced to obey his master, taking Skywalker before Sidious to turn him to the dark side. As the battle between the Empire and Rebels raged on the ground and in space, father and son dueled once more until Skywalker was consumed with rage, striking against Vader when he taunted that his daughter could be turned to the dark side if his son refused. Desiring to replace Vader with his more powerful son, the Emperor subsequently betrayed Vader by ordering the Jedi Knight to take Vader's' place as Sidious's apprentice.[[34]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-34)

Instead of killing his father, however, Skywalker affirmed he was a Jedi, earning the anger of Sidious who tortured him with [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning"). Before Sidious could kill him, however, Vader returned to the light side to save his son, throwing his Sith Master down a reactor shaft to kill him. The defeat and destruction of the Sith at the hands of the now redeemed Jedi Knight Anakin Skywalker, allowed him to fulfill his role as the Chosen One. Dying in his son's arms, the man who was once again Anakin Skywalker became one with the Force, appearing as a Force-spirit to Luke alongside Yoda and Kenobi.[[34]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-34)

### New Republic Era

#### The Mandalorian and the Child

:   "*If you choose the armor, you'll return to your friend, the Mandalorian. However, you will be giving in to attachment to those that you love and forsaking the way of the Jedi. But if you choose the lightsaber, you will be the first student in my academy, and I will train you to be a great Jedi.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker, to Grogu[[32]](#cite_note-Boba_Chapter_6-32)

 [![The Mandalorian Din Djarin became the guardian of Grogu, a youngling of Yoda's species who survived the Great Jedi Purge.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/Precious-Cargo-Card-Trader.png/revision/latest?cb=20210221050730) [![The Mandalorian Din Djarin became the guardian of Grogu, a youngling of Yoda's species who survived the Great Jedi Purge.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/Precious-Cargo-Card-Trader.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210221050730)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/Precious-Cargo-Card-Trader.png/revision/latest?cb=20210221050730) 

The Mandalorian Din Djarin became the guardian of Grogu, a youngling of Yoda's species who survived the Great Jedi Purge.

 

Ahsoka Tano was still alive, helping Sabine Wren on her [search](/wiki/Quest_to_find_Ezra_Bridger "Quest to find Ezra Bridger") for the still-missing Ezra Bridger.[[161]](#cite_note-Family&Farewell-161) Following the fall of the Galactic Empire during the [Battle of Jakku](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku"),[[204]](#cite_note-Aftermath:_Empire's_End-204) an [Imperial remnant](/wiki/Gideon%27s_Imperial_remnant "Gideon's Imperial remnant") led by [Moff](/wiki/Moff "Moff") [Gideon](/wiki/Gideon "Gideon") sought to capture [Grogu](/wiki/Din_Grogu "Din Grogu"), a Force-sensitive infant of [Yoda's species](/wiki/Yoda%27s_species "Yoda's species"), for his blood.[[205]](#cite_note-Chapter_16-205) Before Order 66, Grogu had been a youngling in the Jedi Order before being hidden from the Empire.[[206]](#cite_note-Chapter_13-206) In [9 ABY](/wiki/9_ABY "9 ABY"),[[10]](#cite_note-Timelines-10) the Mandalorian bounty hunter [Din Djarin](/wiki/Din_Djarin "Din Djarin") took the Child as his [foundling](/wiki/Foundling "Foundling"), escaping the remnant and its hired bounty hunters.[[207]](#cite_note-Chapter_3-207) Amid a [clash on Nevarro](/wiki/Clash_on_Nevarro "Clash on Nevarro"), "[the Armorer](/wiki/The_Armorer "The Armorer")" tasked him with returning Grogu to the Jedi after telling him about the Order.[[67]](#cite_note-Chapter_8-67)

After meeting [Lady](/wiki/Lady "Lady") [Bo-Katan Kryze](/wiki/Bo-Katan_Kryze "Bo-Katan Kryze"), Djarin was pointed to Tano,[[208]](#cite_note-Chapter_11-208) who was on the world of [Corvus](/wiki/Corvus "Corvus") to get the location of Grand Admiral Thrawn from [Magistrate](/wiki/Magistrate "Magistrate") [Morgan Elsbeth](/wiki/Morgan_Elsbeth "Morgan Elsbeth"). Although she refused to train Grogu, Tano pointed Djarin to the Jedi planet [Tython](/wiki/Tython "Tython"), where Grogu could be able to reach out to one of the few Jedi left in the galaxy.[[206]](#cite_note-Chapter_13-206) Even though Grogu managed to connect with Luke Skywalker,[[205]](#cite_note-Chapter_16-205) the infant was captured by Gideon's remnant.[[209]](#cite_note-Chapter_14-209) Leading his allies to [rescue Grogu](/wiki/Second_rescue_of_Grogu "Second rescue of Grogu") from [Gideon's light cruiser](/wiki/Gideon%27s_light_cruiser "Gideon's light cruiser"), Djarin and his team found themselves under siege from [Gideon's dark trooper platoon](/wiki/Gideon%27s_Dark_Trooper_platoon "Gideon's Dark Trooper platoon"), only for Skywalker and R2-D2 to arrive in Red Five. Cutting down every [third-generation design Dark Trooper](/wiki/Phase-III_Dark_Trooper "Phase-III Dark Trooper"), Skywalker agreed to train Grogu, departing with the infant and R2.[[205]](#cite_note-Chapter_16-205) Grogu trained with Skywalker for some time at his under-construction [Jedi academy](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_of_Luke_Skywalker "Jedi Temple of Luke Skywalker"), where Tano joined him in watching over the Child's growing abilities.[[32]](#cite_note-Boba_Chapter_6-32) Ultimately, however, Grogu chose to return to Djarin rather than continue down the life of a Jedi.[[210]](#cite_note-Boba_Chapter_7-210)

#### The new generation

:   "*He was training a new generation of Jedi. One boy, an apprentice turned against him, destroyed it all. Luke felt responsible. He just walked away from everything.*"
:   ―Han Solo[[27]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-27)

 [![Skywalker passed on the ways of the Force to a new generation of Jedi, which included his nephew Ben Solo.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/LukeTeachingJedi-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250306232725) [![Skywalker passed on the ways of the Force to a new generation of Jedi, which included his nephew Ben Solo.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/LukeTeachingJedi-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250306232725)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/LukeTeachingJedi-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250306232725) 

Skywalker passed on the ways of the Force to a new generation of Jedi, which included his nephew Ben Solo.

 

Skywalker began to work on rebuilding the Jedi Order after the Galactic Civil War during the [time](/wiki/New_Republic_era "New Republic era") of the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"), eventually gathering a group of Jedi students, among them his nephew, [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo").[[27]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-27) the [Quarren](/wiki/Quarren "Quarren") [Hennix](/wiki/Hennix "Hennix"), and fellow [humans](/wiki/Human "Human") [Tai](/wiki/Tai "Tai") and [Voe](/wiki/Voe "Voe").[[211]](#cite_note-The_Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-211) However, Luke sensed a growing darkness in Ben and eventually went to confront his nephew in the night. When Luke peered into his nephew's mind while he slept, he saw the machinations of the mysterious dark side wielder [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke") and Ben's darkness, which would lead to death, destruction, and despair in the galaxy, and, in a moment of pure instinct, ignited his lightsaber. Luke, whose [family](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family") had a history with the dark side, was quickly overcome by shame and regret, but before he could put away his blade, his nephew woke up, and, in the confusion of the moment, ignited his own lightsaber to clash with his uncle and brought down his hut on him.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-11)

When Ben lashed out against his uncle, he destroyed Skywalker's [Jedi Academy](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_of_Luke_Skywalker "Jedi Temple of Luke Skywalker") along with most of its students.[[212]](#cite_note-USWNE-212) Ben had emerged from the wreckage of his hut enraged about his uncle's actions, but he was horrified when a lightning storm appeared and [razed the temple](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Destruction of the Jedi Temple"). Shortly after that, Hennix, Tai, and Voe returned on their starship *[Verity](/wiki/Verity "Verity")*. Sensing only Ben's presence, they confronted Ben, who told them Skywalker had tried to kill him. In response to Ben's evasive and confrontational behavior, they fought and pursued him. In despair and confusion, Ben turned to his friend Snoke.[[211]](#cite_note-The_Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-211) When Skywalker emerged from the rubble, he saw that Ben had burned the temple, but mistakenly believed that Ben had slaughtered most of his students while taking the rest with him.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-11)

Ben fled the other Jedi students to become Snoke's student and contacted [Ren](/wiki/Ren_(human) "Ren (human)"), the leader of the [Knights of Ren](/wiki/Knights_of_Ren "Knights of Ren"), offering to join the dark siders.[[213]](#cite_note-The_Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-213) Tai, Voe and Hennix cornered Ben on [Elphrona](/wiki/Elphrona "Elphrona"), leading to a [duel](/wiki/Battle_of_Elphrona "Battle of Elphrona") which resulted in Hennix's death. Reaching the Knights of Ren on [Varnak](/wiki/Varnak "Varnak"), Ben was deemed not yet ready by Ren,[[214]](#cite_note-The_Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-214) who allowed him to accompany the group to obtain a Force artifact called the [Mindsplinter](/wiki/Mindsplinter "Mindsplinter") on the [Minemoon](/wiki/Minemoon "Minemoon"). There, Ben succumbed to the dark side when Ren murdered Tai, making him kill Ren and then Voe, thus killing the last remaining Padawan. Now consumed by the dark side of the Force, Ben Solo became Kylo Ren and assumed leadership of the Knights of Ren.[[215]](#cite_note-The_Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_4-215)

### A ray of hope

:   "*The rebellion is reborn today, the war is just beginning, and I will not be the last Jedi.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-11)

 [![Though reluctant to train another apprentice after his nephew's turn to the dark side, Skywalker agreed to teach the Jedi arts to the scavenger Rey.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/Luke_training_Rey.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200626064527) [![Though reluctant to train another apprentice after his nephew's turn to the dark side, Skywalker agreed to teach the Jedi arts to the scavenger Rey.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/Luke_training_Rey.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20200626064527)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/Luke_training_Rey.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200626064527) 

Though reluctant to train another apprentice after his nephew's turn to the dark side, Skywalker agreed to teach the Jedi arts to the scavenger Rey.

 

Sometime later, as [war](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War") erupted between the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order") and the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance") for control of the galaxy, an orphaned [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") named [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") approached Luke at the first Jedi Temple on Ahch-To, seeking to be trained as a Jedi, having been sent by General Leia Organa, leader of the Resistance, Luke's sister, and Kylo Ren's mother. Though Luke rejected her at first, he eventually agreed to train her. A Force bond that connected Kylo Ren and Rey brought her to the *[Supremacy](/wiki/Supremacy "Supremacy")*, where Kylo turned her over to his master, [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") Snoke. However, Kylo killed his master, and fought with Rey against his [Elite Praetorian Guard](/wiki/Praetorian_Guard "Praetorian Guard").[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-11)

When Kylo usurped his master's power, Rey abandoned him and joined with the fleeing Resistance on [Crait](/wiki/Crait "Crait"), where the [Battle of Crait](/wiki/Battle_of_Crait "Battle of Crait") had erupted. As Rey helped the few Resistance survivors escape aboard the *[Millennium Falcon](/wiki/Millennium_Falcon "Millennium Falcon")*, inspired by Rey to new faith in the Jedi and the goodness of their cause, Luke projected an image of himself on Crait to distract Kylo Ren and the First Order. He warned Kylo that he would not be the last Jedi, naming Rey his successor, before becoming one with the Force. Luke's tale went on to spread across the galaxy as a symbol of hope in a dark time as the First Order rose to power.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-11) When Darth Sidious was revealed to be resurrected in the [year](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY") following the Battle at Crait, Rey, who had continued her [Jedi training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") under Leia Organa, and her companions in the Resistance undertook a [series](/wiki/Mission_to_Pasaana_(Resistance) "Mission to Pasaana (Resistance)") [of](/wiki/Mission_to_Kijimi "Mission to Kijimi") [missions](/wiki/Mission_to_Kef_Bir "Mission to Kef Bir") to find a way to safely navigate through space to Exegol, where Sidious's [lair](/wiki/Sith_Citadel "Sith Citadel") and his [followers](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal") were located.[[216]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-216)

 [![Rey hears the voices of late Jedi while facing Darth Sidious during the Battle of Exegol.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/RiseSkywalkeradaption-voices-of-Jedi-past.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913172513) [![Rey hears the voices of late Jedi while facing Darth Sidious during the Battle of Exegol.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/RiseSkywalkeradaption-voices-of-Jedi-past.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220913172513)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/RiseSkywalkeradaption-voices-of-Jedi-past.png/revision/latest?cb=20220913172513) 

Rey hears the voices of late Jedi while facing Darth Sidious during the Battle of Exegol.

 

After learning from Kylo Ren that Darth Sidious was her grandfather and that she was a [Palpatine](/wiki/Palpatine_family "Palpatine family"), Rey briefly considered exiling herself at the first Jedi Temple as her old master had, but the spirit of Skywalker appeared before Rey to encourage her to confront her fear, teaching his student that it was the destiny of all Jedi and that he had been wrong about his self-imposed exile. Rey and a redeemed Kylo Ren, who renounced the dark side and reclaimed his birth identity Ben Solo, confronted Sidious during a [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol") at Exegol. Sidious used their bond as a [Force dyad](/wiki/Force_dyad "Force dyad") to rejuvenate himself, but Rey was restrengthened when she reached out to and heard the voices of the past Jedi, allowing her to stand reflect his lightning to destroy Sidious and the Sith for good. Rey was killed as a result of the ensuring explosion, but she was revived when Solo gave his life for hers. Although the [Skywalker bloodline](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family") ended, their actions allowed the Jedi to prevail and prevent the return of the Sith. Rey chose to adopt the surname "Skywalker" when she visited the [Lars Homestead](/wiki/Lars_homestead "Lars homestead") on Tatooine and saw the spirits of Luke and Leia in the distance.[[216]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-216)

In the aftermath of the First Order/Resistance War, Rey eventually gained the status of Jedi Master. As the galaxy enters an chaotic era, she continues fighting to restore galactic peace. As Master, Rey started to work on rebuilding the Jedi.[[142]](#cite_note-TSWB-142)

## Jedi ranks

### Main ranks

:   "*After successfully passing a rigorous series of tests that challenged mind, body, and spirit, a Padawan became a bona fide Jedi Knight, a shining symbol of peace and justice across the galaxy.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker[[51]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-51)

Members of the Jedi Order held various positions within the Order at times as they studied the Force and gained experience.[[25]](#cite_note-Convergence-25) These ranks included:

 [![A Padawan was a Jedi apprentice who trained to become a full-fledged Jedi Knight.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/36/AnakinSkywalkerEpII-SWBC52.png/revision/latest?cb=20240106054948) [![A Padawan was a Jedi apprentice who trained to become a full-fledged Jedi Knight.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/36/AnakinSkywalkerEpII-SWBC52.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20240106054948)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/36/AnakinSkywalkerEpII-SWBC52.png/revision/latest?cb=20240106054948) 

A Padawan was a Jedi apprentice who trained to become a full-fledged Jedi Knight.

 

* **[Jedi Initiate](/wiki/Jedi_Initiate "Jedi Initiate")**: A young child who was Force-sensitive would be identified at birth and taken to the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") on Coruscant to be trained as a Jedi.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1) They were to be put into classes of other Jedi younglings[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_II-5) and trained together before being taken as an apprentice by a [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight").[[104]](#cite_note-Clone_Wars_film-104) Younglings were not to be trained once they had reached a certain age, with the sole exception to this rule being Anakin Skywalker.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1) Younglings would participate in [the Gathering](/wiki/Gathering "Gathering"), which was the pilgrimage to the [Ilum](/wiki/Ilum "Ilum") [Temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_(Ilum) "Jedi Temple (Ilum)") to gain a kyber crystal for their [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber").[[217]](#cite_note-The_Gathering-217)
* **[Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan")**: A youngling who had been chosen by a Jedi Knight or Jedi Master to train under their tutelage personally into becoming a fully fledged Jedi Knight. Their readiness was decided by the [Initiate Trials](/wiki/Initiate_Trials "Initiate Trials"). Padawans wore a [braid](/wiki/Padawan_braid "Padawan braid").[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1)
* **[Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight")**: Once a Padawan has successfully passed the [Jedi trials](/wiki/Jedi_Trials "Jedi Trials"), they were be granted the rank of Jedi Knight and went out on missions of their own, no longer under the tutelage of a master and may take on a Padawan themselves.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1)
* **[Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master")**: A Jedi Knight was granted the rank of Jedi Master when they had proven themselves. A select few masters were offered a seat on the Jedi High Council when they had shown great skill, wisdom and devotion to the Force.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_I-1) Some Masters became [Sage Masters](/wiki/Sage_Master "Sage Master") or [Warrior Masters](/wiki/Jedi_Guardian "Jedi Guardian").[[3]](#cite_note-CL-3)
* **[Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master")**: The leader of the Jedi High Council, the position of Grand Master was given to the oldest and considered to be the wisest member of the Jedi Order.[[218]](#cite_note-Yoda_DB-218)

### Jedi occupations

:   "*I've trained all my life to understand the call of the Force. Through that understanding, I can serve the galaxy, whether as a lone Wayseeker or by taking on an apprentice.*"
:   ―[Gella Nattai](/wiki/Gella_Nattai "Gella Nattai")[[25]](#cite_note-Convergence-25)

Some members of the Jedi Order had specific titles and roles within the Order. These included:

 [![Master of the Order was the title of the Jedi who assumed leadership over the Jedi Council.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Masters_of_the_Order.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150926110104) [![Master of the Order was the title of the Jedi who assumed leadership over the Jedi Council.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Masters_of_the_Order.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20150926110104)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Masters_of_the_Order.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150926110104) 

Master of the Order was the title of the Jedi who assumed leadership over the Jedi Council.

 

* **[Jedi Advisor](/wiki/Jedi_Advisor "Jedi Advisor")**: A Jedi who worked as a personal [advisor](/wiki/Advisor "Advisor").[[219]](#cite_note-Unlimited_Power-219)
* **[Master of the Order](/wiki/Master_of_the_Order "Master of the Order")**: This position was assumed by the leader of the Jedi High Council.[[220]](#cite_note-Insider_199-220) They had to be voted unanimously into the position by the council's members.[[221]](#cite_note-AbEverything-221)
* **[Jedi Temple Guard](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_Guard "Jedi Temple Guard")**: Headed by [Cin Drallig](/wiki/Cin_Drallig "Cin Drallig") during the Clone Wars, these anonymous Jedi guarded the Jedi Temple with [lightsaber pikes](/wiki/Lightsaber_pike "Lightsaber pike").[[222]](#cite_note-JTG_DB-222)
* **[Jedi investigator](/wiki/Jedi_investigator "Jedi investigator")**: These Jedi were [detectives](/wiki/Detective "Detective") who aided [police](/wiki/Law_enforcement_agency "Law enforcement agency") with the use of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force").[[223]](#cite_note-Tera_Sinube-223) They also used [crime scene analysis droids](/wiki/SP-4_ISC_crime_scene_analysis_droid "SP-4 ISC crime scene analysis droid").[[224]](#cite_note-Russo-ISC_Databank-224)
* **[Consular Jedi](/wiki/Consular_Jedi "Consular Jedi")**: These Jedi devoted themselves to the study of diplomacy or science and avoided combat and warfare duties.[[225]](#cite_note-TVE-225)
* **[Chief Librarian](/wiki/Chief_Librarian "Chief Librarian")**: This Jedi oversaw the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives "Jedi Archives") and [Holocron Vault](/wiki/Holocron_Vault "Holocron Vault").[[226]](#cite_note-Jocasta_Nu_DB-226)
* **[Jedi seeker](/wiki/Jedi_seeker "Jedi seeker")**: These Jedi searched the galaxy for Force-sensitive children in order to recruit them into the Jedi Order.[[227]](#cite_note-Jedi_Lost-227)
* **[Jedi Sentinel](/wiki/Jedi_Sentinel "Jedi Sentinel")**: Jedi who focused on small-scale, community matters.[[228]](#cite_note-Endless_Vigil-228)
* **[Jedi Guardian](/wiki/Jedi_Guardian "Jedi Guardian")**:[[228]](#cite_note-Endless_Vigil-228) Jedi also known as "Warrior Masters."[[229]](#cite_note-CL2016-229)
* **[Jedi Wayseeker](/wiki/Wayseeker "Wayseeker")**: Jedi of the High Republic Era who operated independently from the Jedi High Council and followed only the will of the Force.[[49]](#cite_note-Into_the_Dark-49)

### Jedi military ranks

:   "*The general is the one who gives the orders around here.*"
:   ―Clone Commander [Grey](/wiki/Grey_(clone_trooper) "Grey (clone trooper)") rebukes Clone Sergeant [Hunter](/wiki/Hunter "Hunter"), referring to Jedi General [Depa Billaba](/wiki/Depa_Billaba "Depa Billaba")[[230]](#cite_note-Aftermath-230)

At the onset of the Clone Wars, the Jedi, the guardians of peace and justice in the Galactic Republic, were chosen by the Galactic Senate, whom the Jedi owed their allegiance to,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_III-9) to lead the new Grand Army of the Republic. They were thus given either of the respective ranks in the [Republic Military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military"):

* **[Jedi Commander](/wiki/Jedi_Commander "Jedi Commander")**: Granted to Padawans, who served as second-in-commands to Jedi Generals in the Grand Army of the Republic.[[104]](#cite_note-Clone_Wars_film-104)
* **[Jedi General](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General")**: Granted to Jedi Knights and Jedi Masters, who served as the highest ranking [officers](/wiki/Officer "Officer") within the Grand Army of the Republic.[[3]](#cite_note-CL-3)
